Zalisa ezi fom zesicelo zilandelayo : .
Yenza isicelo sokubeka igama ngokuhambisa i - Isicelo sokubeka igama . .
Le fom iyafumaneka kwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini . .
Zalisa i - Imiba equlathwe yirejista equlathe iinkcukacha zabalawuli kunye namagosa . .
Le fom iyafumaneka kwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini . .
Umlalwuli ngamnye wenkampani kufuneka azalise ifom ye . .
Le fom iyafumaneka kwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini . .
Zalisa ifom ekuthiwa yi ukuze unike imvume yomntu ozakubamba isikhundla somphicothi weencwadi zemali . .
Le fom iyafumaneka kwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini . .
Zalisa ifom ekuthiwa yi - Imimiselo yeQumrhu lenkampani elinobutyebi bezinto kunye neemali zezabelo ezinoluhlu lomgaqo osisihlomelo 1 , okanye ifom ekuthiwa yi - Imimiselo yeQumrhu lenkampani elinobutyebi bezinto kunye neemali zezabelo ezingenaluhlu lomgaqo osisihlomelo 1 . .
Bonke abalawuli kufuneka bazalise ifom ekuthiwa yi - Abantu abasayine iMimiselo .
Nika igqwetha incwadi egunyazisiweyo yamandla egqwetha , echaza ukuba ulinika igunya lokuba likumele . .
Iinkampani ezibhalisa ngemali eyinkunzi ( imali yokuqalisa ) kukwafuneka zikhuphe le miqulu ilandelayo : .
CM1 : Isatifiketi sokuseka inkampani ngokwasemthethweni .
Lo ngumqulu osayinwa kwaye ugximfizwe isitampu nguMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani xa sele yonke imiqulu ehamba nesicelo ( njengoko idwelisiwe apha ngasentla ) ijongiwe kwaze kwagqitywa ngayo . .
I : UMqulu oBhaliweyo wequmrhu kudityaniswe - i - i - i ukuba ngaba abantu abanezabelo bangaphezulu kwe 1 okanye 2D ukuba ngaba mnye umntu onezabelo .
UMthetho weMitshato yeSiko leSiqhelo wabangumthetho ngomhla we 15 Novemba 2000 . .
Ukubangaba wawukumtshato owawukhona nowawusebenziseka phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo phambi kwalo mhla , umtshato wakho uyavunywa phantsi kwalo mthetho mtsha . .
Lo mthetho ukwayivuma imitshato engenelwe emva kwalo mhla , kwaye uchaza imigaqo ekufuneka ilandelwe ngabantu abatshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo ukuze imitshato yabo ivunywe . .
Umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo uyavunywa ukuba ngaba abantu abatshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo bahambisene nezi mfuneko zilandelayo : .
Bobabini aba bantu batshatayo kufuneka babengaphezulu kweminyaka elishumi elinesibhozo ubudala .
Bobabini kufuneka bavume ukutshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo .
Umtshato kufuneka kuthetha ngawo , kuvuyiswane ngawo kwaye ungenelwe ngokuhambisana nomthetho wesiko lesiqhelo .
Ilobola ayingomba oyimfuneko ukuze umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo usebenziseke .
Qaphela ukuba le mitshato kudala ivunywa phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo . .
Ndiwubhalisa nini umtshato wam ? .
Ukubangaba watshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo phambi komhla we 15 Novemba 2000 , umtshato wakho kufanele ubhaliswe kwiSebe lezeKhaya . .
Ukubangaba watshata emva kokuba umthetho uwisiwe , kufanele ubhalise umtshato wakho kwisithuba seenyanga ezintathu emva komtshato . .
IMitshato yeSiko leSiqhelo kunye nenkqubo yokuDityanelwa kweMpahla neZinto kunye naMatyala .
Yonke imitshato yesiko lesiqhelo engenelwe emva kokuqalisa kokusebenza koMthetho , ikwinkqubo yokudityanelwa kwempahla nezinto kunye namatyala . .
Oku kuthetha ukuba umyeni nenkosikazi yakhe bahlulelana ngokulinganayo kwizinto abanazo , imali kunye nempahla , kwaye ikwathetha ukuba bahlulelana ngawo onke amatyala . .
Ukubangaba aba bantu babini bangathanda ukuba umtshato wabo ubengaphandle kwenkqubo yokudityanelwa kwempahla nezinto kunye namatyala , kuyakufuneka bangenele isivumelwano sekhontrakthi yokuba umntu ngamnye agcine izinto ezizezakhe , phambi kokuba batshate . .
Ukubangaba bafuna ukutshintsha emva kokuba sele betshatile , kuyakufuneka benze isicelo kwiNkundla ePhakamileyo . .
Phantsi koMthetho weMitshato yeSiko leSiqhelo , inkosikazi inelungelo elilinganayo kunye nobume obulinganayo nomyeni wayo bokwenza isigqibo ngomakwenzeke kwimpahla nezinto zabo . .
Ngoku inkosikazi yesiko lesiqhelo inamandla okungenela isivumelwano sekhontrakthi ngaphandle kokuncediswa ngumyeni wayo . .
Ndenza njani xa ngaba umyeni wam ufuna ukutshata omnye umfazi ? .
Umyeni kufuneka angenele isivumelwano esibhaliweyo / ikhontrakthi ebhaliweyo eyakuchaza ukuba kuyakwenzeka ntoni na empahleni nakwizinto , kwaye ke futhi umyeni kufuneka enze isicelo enkundleni sokuba ivume ikhontrakthi ebhaliweyo . .
Inkundla kufanele iqinisekise ukuba zonke iimfuno zempahla nezinto zabo bonke abafazi , ziyakhuselwa . .
Senza njani xa ngaba sifuna ukungenela umtshato wentlalo yoluntu emva kokutshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo ? .
Ukubangaba umyeni akanabafazi abangabanye , ungatshata phantsi komthetho wentlalo yoluntu ndawonye naphantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo . .
Kodwa ke , akukho namnye phakathi kwenu oyakubanako ukungenela imitshato yesiko lesiqhelo naye nabanina omnye ngelilixa nitshate phantsi komthetho wentlalo yoluntu . .
Umyeni okanye inkosikazi , angabhalisa umtshato kwiSebe lezeKhaya elikufuphi kuye . .
Kulicebo elihle ukuba bobabini abalingane bayokubhalisa umtshato bebobabini ukuze ubhaliso lukhawuleze . .
Kodwa ke , ukuba ngaba omnye umlingane uyala , ungabhalisa ngokwakho uze ke uphathe ubungqina obuyimfuneko . .
Phatha incwadi yakho yesazisi ( ID ) , uze ugcwalise iFom A , ethi : Isicelo sobhaliso lomtshato wesiko lesiqhelo / ukubuzisa ngobukho bomtshato wesiko lesiqhelo , ekufuna ukuba unike le nkcazelo ilandelayo : .
iinombolo ze , amagama kunye nemihla yokuzalwa yomyeni nenkosikazi .
amagama wabazali bomyeni kunye nabenkosikazi kunye negama lenkokeli yemveli okanye amagama eenkokeli zemveli .
iinkcukacha zesivumelwano selobola / magadi , kunye .
nabantu ababini abangamangqina omtshato ( ingqina elinye kufuneka limele umyeni lize elinye limele inkosikazi ) .
incwadi esuka kwinkokeli yemveli okanye incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo ( i ) .
Ifom kufuneka ingqinwe kwaye isayinwe phambi : .
kwegosa elibhalisayo , okanye .
umntu ochongelwe ukwenza lo msebenzi , ochongelwe wona nguMqondisi ukuze enze imisebenzi ngokwale migqaliselo . .
Isicelo kufuneka sifakwe kwigosa elibhalisayo okanye kumntu ochongelwe ukwenza loo msebenzi , ekufuneka yena akunike incwadi evuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo ngokweFom B , ethi : Ukuvuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo sobhaliso lomtshato wesiko lesiqhelo .
Igosa lobhaliso okanye umntu ochongelwe ukwenza lo msebenzi uyakusa isicelo kwi yengingqi okanye yesithili ekufuphi yeSebe ukuze sifakwe kwincwadi yobhaliso lwenani neenkcukacha zabantu . .
Uyakunikwa isatifiketi sobhaliso okanye iFom C , ethi : Isatifiketi somtshato wesiko lesiqhelo . .
Gcina isatifiketi kwindawo ekhuselekileyo kuba sibalulekile . .
Inqanawa yokuloba yelizwe langaphandle yinqanawa yommi ongengowaseMzantsi Afrika , o.k.t. ummi welizwe langaphandle kwaye ibhaliswe phantsi kwelinye iLizwe elinegunya lolawulo lwale nqanawa elingeyiyo iRiphabliki yoMzantsi Afrika . .
Kuphela iba ziimeko ezingenakulawuleka ezibangela ukuba inqanawa elolu hlobo inikwe amalungelo okanye ibenemvumelwano yoMnikazi waseMzantsi Afrika oneLungelo ukuba yenze imisebenzi yokuloba kummandla okhethekileyo okanye amanzi amazwe ngamazwe phantsi kweflegi yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Akukho nqanawa yelinye ilizwe iya kukhutshelwa ilayisenisi yaseMzantsi Afrika yokuloba ngaphandle kokuba iloba ihlangene nomnye uMnikazi waseMzantsi Afrika onelayisenisi yokuloba . .
Ngaphambi kokuqalisa imisebenzi yokuloba , makuqhagamshelwane neSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho , ukuqinisekisa ukuba ngaba ukunikwa imvume yokuloba kwenqanawa yokuloba kuya kuvumeleka kwelo candelo lithe ngqo lokuloba kwaye ngawaphi na amaxwebhu ayimfuneko ukulungiselela ukuvunywa kwesicelo esilolu hlobo . .
Xa ngaba ngokomqathango kunikwa inkxaso ukusetyenziswa kwenqanawa lelinye ilizwe , umenzi kufuneka ukuba afumane ifom yokwenza isicelo selayisenisi yokuloba yenqanawa yelizwe langaphandle kwi ekufutshane yeSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho . .
Zalisa ifom yokwenza isicelo uze uyingenise kwi ekufutshane kunye nawe yakwa kunye nale ngcaciso ilandelayo : .
igama lenqanawa yokuloba .
igama neenkcukacha zenqanawa zomnikazi wenqanawa ( kubandakanywa nezabelo zobunini ukuba yinqanawa ekudityenwe ngayo kunye ngabemi belizwe langaphandle kunye nabemi boMzantsi Afrika ) .
umlinganiselo wamandla e yenqanawa .
ubude nomthamo wenqanawa .
inombolo yokubhalisa yenqanawa .
ilizwe elinegunya lolawulo inqanawa ebhaliswe phantsi kwalo njengangoku ukuba ( inikwe imvume yokuloba kulo okanye yeyabemi baseMzantsi Afrika abangabanini ngokuhlangeneyo ) . .
isatifikethi esisemthethweni sokhuseleko esivela kwiLizwe i State .
Inqanawa yokuloba iyakwenziwa inkqubo iyakuvavanyelwa ukulungela iimeko zolwandle yi African Maritime Safety Authority ( SAMSA ) ngeendleko zomnikazi nqanawa . .
Zonke iinqanawa zamazwe angaphandle ziyacelwa ukuba zibe ne C VMS esebenzayo apho kuzo ngaphakathi nenika ingxelo kubaLawuli boLwandle noNxweme . .
Oku makungqinisiswe licandelo i and Coastal Management's VMS Operations Section . .
Kwisicelo sakho , bonisa icandelo lokuloba apho inqanawa iya kusebenza khona kwakunye nexesha lokusebenza kwayo . .
Ileta esemthethweni evela kwi State's Fisheries Authority iya kufuneka , nemvume yokuba : .
inqanawa ivunyelwe ukuloba kumanzi aseMzantsi Afrika .
inqanawa ayizange nangaliphi na ithuba ibe yinxalenye yomsebenzi wobugwenxa ongekho mthethweni nongenamiqathango .
i African Fisheries Authority iya kuthwala uxanduva lokulawula le nqanawa .
i African Fisheries Authority iya kuthwala uxanduva lokunika ingxelo malunga neentlanzi ezilotyiweyo kwi Fisheries Management Organisations ( RFMOs ) ukuba akuyomfuneko oko .
ngokwe , iinkcukacha ngeentlanzi ezilotyiweyo xa zizonke , nokuba ngaba kulapha ngaphakathi kummandla woMzantsi Afrika okanye kwii Seas , eziya kufunyanwa eMzantsi Afrika ngethuba lokunikwa imvume yokuloba , ukuze .
inqanawa yelizwe langaphandle iya kuloba phantsi kwemigaqo yoMzantsi Afrika neemeko zepemithi . .
Ukuba inqanawa ayiyonqanawa ityunjiweyo ngokumalunga nenkqubo yokwabelwa amalungelo ( in terms of the rights allocation process ) ngoko ke umenzi kufuneka azalise ifom yokutshintshwa kwenqanawa . .
Ukuze inqanawa ibenegunya lokuloba umenzi kungafuneka azalise ifom yepemithi yokuloba ngokwecandelo inqanawa eza kuloba kulo . .
Okokugqibela , ukuba umenzi unqwenela ukuba inqanawa ingaloba kummandla we Seas ngethuba lokunikwa imvume , ngoko ke kusafuneka ukuba kuzaliswe ifom yokwenza isicelo ye Seas . .
Inkqubo yoKwaba Ngokutsha uMhlaba wokuPhuhlisa eZolimo , ekuthiwa yi Redistribution for Agricultural Development ( LRAD ) , yaqingqelwa ukunceda abemi ababekade bedlelwa indlala abangabahlali abaNtsundu , abangamaKhaladi kunye nabangamaNdiya ukuze bathenge umhlaba okanye izixhobo zezolimo ngeenjongo ezingqale nqo kwezolimo . .
Ukuze uvumeleke , kufuneka .
ube ungumntu owayekade edlelwa indlala ( oko kukuthi uNtsundu , uliKhaladi okanye uliNdiya ) .
ubeneminyaka yobudala eli 18 okanye ngaphezulu .
ube ujonge ukusebenzisa umhlaba ngeenjongo zezolimo kuphela .
ube ujonge ukuba ngumfama ngokupheleleyo .
ube awunasikhundla osibambileyo kumacandelo karhulumente .
uzimisele ukuthabatha inxaxheba kwinkqubo yoqeqesho emva kokuba ufumene umhlaba .
ubekwimeko yokuba ungenza igalelo .
ubeliqumrhu elakhiwe ngokwamacandelo ukuba ngaba nenza isicelo ningumbutho , kwaye .
ube ne yebhanki . .
Amafama aphumeleleyo anqwenela ukwandisa iinkqubo zawo angenza ezinye izicelo zegranti , kodwa igranti epheleleyo ye kumenzi omnye akufanelanga igqithe kwi 000 . .
Enye imali eyinkunzi yokuqalisa okanye yokwandisa iprojekthi yokufama kufuneka ifunyanwe ebhankini . .
Chaza umhlaba ofuna ukuwuthenga . .
Kungenjalo , mhlawumbi sele unawo umhlaba , ofana nomhlaba onabanikazi abawudibaneleyo . .
Nxulumana neSebe lezeMihlaba okanye igosa lendawo ohlala kuyo lesihlomelo sezolimo ukuze wenze isicelo segranti . .
Hambisa le miqulu ilandelayo nesicelo sakho : .
umpoposho wokusebenzisa umhlaba okanye isicwangciso sokufama ( umpoposho weprojekthi ) .
indlela yokukhetha ukuthengisa ngexabiso ekuvunyelwene ngalo ukuba ngaba ungenela isivumelwano sengqeshiso esinendlela yokukhetha ukuthenga .
uluhlu lwamalungu ekhaya okanye amalungu ombutho , ukuba ngaba umpoposho ngowombutho .
ingxelo yokuphonononga ixabiso .
ISAHLUKO SOKU .
INTSHAYELELO .
UKWAZISA INKCAZELO YEKHARITYHULAMU YESIZWE .
UMgaqo weRiphablikhi yoMzantsi Afrika yonyaka ka1996 ( uMthetho we we ) unika isiseko sokuguqula nokuphuhlisa ikharityhulamu kuMzantsi Afrika wanamhla . .
Intshayelelo yoMgaqo ichaza ukuba iinjongo zoMgaqo kuku : .
phelisa iiyantlukwano zangaphambili kwaye kuzinziswe uluntu olusekwe kukuxabiseka kwesizwe esilawulwa yintando yesininzi , kubulungisa bentlalo namalungelo oluntu asisiseko . .
phucula umgangatho wobomi wabemi bonke nokukhulula amandla aleleyo omntu ngamnye . .
enza isiseko soluntu solawulo nesivulekileyo apho urhulumente usekeke kwintando yabantu kwaye wonke ummi ukhuselwe ngokulinganayo ngumthetho . .
akha uMzantsi Afrika olawulwa yintando yesininzi omanyeneyo okwaziyo ukuthatha indawo elungileyo njengombuso ozimeleyo kumnombo wezizwe . .
Imfundo nekharityhulamu zinendima ebalulekileyo eziyidlalayo ekuphumezeni ezi njongo . .
Ikharityhulamu inenjongo yokuphuhlisa ngokupheleleyo amandla aleleyo omfundi ngamnye njengommi woMzantsi Afrika olawulwa yintando yesininzi . .
Imfundo esekeke kwiziPhumo .
Imfundo esekeke kwiziphumo yakha isiseko sekharityhulamu eMzantsi Afrika . .
Izama ukwenza ukuba bonke abafundi baphumelele kowona mgangatho wabo wobuchule uphezulu . .
Oku kwenziwa ngokumisela iziphumo emaziphunyelelwe ekupheleni kwenkqubo . .
Iziphumo zikhuthaza inkqubo yemfundo ejolise kumfundi nakwimisebenzi . .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo yakha iziphumo zezifundo zeBakala leMfundo noQeqesho Jikelele zamaBanga ukusuka kuLwamkelo ukuya kwele ( ezikolo ) kwiziphumo ezingundoqo nakweziphuhlisayo . .
Iziphumo ezingundoqo zilindela abafundi abaza kukwazi uku .
chonga nokusombulula iingxaki nokwenza izigqibo besebenzisa ingcinga enzulu neqiqayo ; .
sebenza ngokufanelekileyo nabanye , njengamalungu eqela , imibutho noluntu ; .
ukuzicwangcisa nokuzilawula becwangcisa kwaye belawula nemisebenzi yabo ngokuthembekileyo nangokufanelekiyo ; .
qokelela , ukuhlalutya , ukucwangcisa nokuvavanya ulwazi ngokunzulu ; .
nxibelelana ngokufanelekileyo besebenzisa ubuchule bokubonwayo , bemiqondiso no / okanye bolwimi kwimizekelo eyahlukeneyo ; .
sebenzisa inzululwazi neteknoloji ngokufanelekileyo , bebonakalisa ngokunzulu iimfanelo kummandla nempilo yabanye ; .
bonisa ingqiqo yelizwe njengoluhlu lwezixokelelwano ezinxulumeneyo ngokunakana ukuba iimeko zokusombulula iingxaki azenzeki ngokwahlukeneyo . .
Imibandela efana nobuhlwempu , ukungalingani , ubuhlanga , isini , ubudala , ukukhubazeka , nemiceli mingeni efana neHIV / AIDS yonke iphembelela iqondo nendlela apho abafundi bangathabatha ngayo inxaxheba ekufundeni . INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo yamaBanga ukusuka kwibanga loLwamkelo ukuya kwele isebenzisa inkqubo edibeneyo yokumisela ubuncinane beemfuno zabafundi bonke . Zonke iiNkcazelo zeeNkalo zeziFundo zizama ukuyila ingqiqo yolwalamano phakathi kobulungisa bentlalo , amalungelo oluntu , ummandla ophilileyo , nokuqukana . Bonke abafundi bakhuthazwa ukwandisa ulwazi , nengqiqo yokwahlukana kobutyebi beli lizwe , ukuquka nezakhiwo zenkcubeko , zenkolo nobuhlanga kule yantlukwano . .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo : IiNkcazelo zeeNkalo zeziFundo .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo yamaBanga ukusuka kwibanga loLwamkelo ukuya kwele iqulathe le Nkcazelo Jikelele neNkcazelo yeeNkalo zeziFundo ezisibhozo : .
IiLwimi .
IMathematika .
INzululwazi ngezoBugqi .
INzululwazi ngezeNtlalo .
UbuGcisa neNkcubeko .
IsiFundo ngezoBomi .
INzululwazi ngezoQoqosho noLawulo .
ITeknoloji .
INkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo nganye ichaza iziPhumo zeziFundo ezingundoqo ekufuneka ziphunyelelwe ekupheleni kweBanga le . .
INkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo nganye ichaza imiGangatho yokuHlola iya kwenza iziPhumo zesifundo ziphunyelelwe . .
ImiGangatho yokuHlola yeyebanga ngalinye kwaye ichaza ububanzi nobunzulu ekufuneka abafundi bekwazile kwaye bakwazi ukukwenza . .
ImiGangatho yokuHlola yeNkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo nganye ibonisa indlela ukukhula kwengqiqo nobuchule okunokwenzeka ngayo ekuhambeni kwexesha . .
ImiGangatho yokuHlola inokuhlanganiswa kumabanga nangokudibene ngokweeNkalo zeziFundo ( apho kuyimfuneko nakwimfundo elungileyo ) nakwingqiqo yenkqubela ngokwamabanga kusembindini wale kharityhulamu . .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo : IiNkqubo zokuFunda .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo ijolise ekuphuculeni ukuzibophelela nobuchule phakathi kootitshala abaya kuba noxanduva lokuphuhlisa iiNkqubo zokuFunda zabo . .
Ukuze kuxhaswe le nkqubo , iSebe leMfundo liya kunika izikhokelo zemigaqo esekeke kwiNkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo nganye . .
Amaphondo aya kuphuhlisa ezinye izikhokelo apho kuyimfuneko ukumelana neyantlukwano . .
Imigaqo ezizisekelo nokuxabiseka kweeNkcazelo zeeNkalo zezifundo zeNkcazelo zeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo zisekela iiNkqubo zokuFunda . .
Ekubeni iiNkalo zeziFundo zichaza iingqiqo , ubuchule , nokuxabiseka ekufuneka ziphunyelelwe ngokwebanga ngokwebanga , iiNkqubo zokuFunda zona zichaza ububanzi bemisebenzi yokufunda nokuhlola yesigaba ngasinye . .
IiNkqubo zokuFunda ziqulathe izintlu zemisebenzi ezinika isantya nolandelelwano lwale misebenzi kunyaka ngamnye , nemizekelo yokuqulunqwa kwezifundo enokuzalisekiswa naninina . .
KwisiGaba esisiSeko kukho iinkqubo zokufunda ezintathu ezizezi : iLitheresi , ukukwazi ukusebenzisa amaNani nezakhono zoBomi . .
KwisiGaba esiPhakathi iiLwimi , neMathematika zisale zizinkqubo zokufunda ezizimeleyo . .
Ezinye iiNkalo zeziFundo zingahlanganiswa ngamaphondo ngemvume yamasebe emfundo yamaphondo . .
Amaphondo anegunya lokuphuhlisa izigqibo ezibanzi ngokwephondo kuhlanganiso lwesiGaba esiPhakathi . .
KwisiGaba esiPhakamileyo kukho iinkqubo zokufunda ezisibhozo ezisekeke kwiiNkalo zeziFundo . .
Ixesha elabelwe iNkalo yesiFundo nganye lalathelwe onke amaBanga neziGaba . .
Ukwabiwa kweXesha .
NgokwesiQendu soMthetho weNgqesho weeTitshala , ( 1998 ) , iimini zesikolo ezisesikweni zootitshala ziya kuba yimizuzu esixhenxe . .
NgokoMthetho woMgaqo weMfundo yeSizwe , ( 1996 ) , ixesha lokufundisa elisesikweni ngeveki liziyure ezingama - 35 . .
Oku kumiselwe kwi : .
1 . Xwebhu lweNkcazelo Jikelele ISBN 1 iphepha le .
2 . Government Gazette No . 23406 , Vol. 443 Meyi 2002 . .
Amaphepha ama nama . .
UHlolo .
INkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo nganye iqulathe icandelo ngeenkcukacha zohlolo . .
Isakhelo semfundo esekeke kwiziphumo isebenzisa iimethodi zohlolo ezivumela iimeko ezahlukeneyo . .
Uhlolo kufuneka lunike izalathisi zokuphunyelelwa ngumfundi kwimeko efanelekileyo necoselelekileyo kwaye luqinisekise ukuba abafundi bahlanganisa ubuchule kwaye babusebenzise . .
Uhlolo kufuneka lwakhe luncede abafundi ukwenza izigwebo malunga nabakwenzayo , bamisele iinjongo zenkqubela nokuqhubela phambili ukufunda . .
UHlobo oluLindelekileyo lweTitshala .
Ootitshala kuyo yonke imigangatho ngabanikeli abaphambili ekuguqulweni kwemfundo eMzantsi Afrika . .
INkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo yamaBanga ukusuka ku ukuya kwele ( eziKolo ) inembono yetitshala oqeqeshiweyo , enobuchule , ozinikeleyo nonenkathalo . .
Baya kukwazi ukuphumelelisa iindima ezahlukeneyo ezikwimiGangatho neziLinganiselo zootitshala . .
Oku kuquka ootitshala njengabalamli bemfundo , abatoliki , abayili beenkqubo zezifundo , nezixhobo zokufunda , iinkokheli , abalawuli , oomanejali , abafundi , abaphandi nabafundi abafunda ubomi bonke , amalungu oluntu , abemi , abacebisi , abahloli neencutshe zenkalo yesifundo / yesigaba . .
UHlobo oluLindelekileyo lomFundi . .
Ukuphuculwa kokuxabiseka akubalulekanga kuphela ekuziphuhliseni , kubaluleke nakukuqinisekisa ukuba ubunguwe ngokobuzwe boMzantsi Afrika bakhelwe kukuxabiseka okwahlukileyo koko kwakuxhasa imfundo yocalu . .
Uhlobo lomfundi olulindelweyo ngulowo oza kuzaliswa koku kuxabiseka noya kusebenza kumdla woluntu ngokusekeke kwintlonelo yesizwe esilawulwa yintando yesininzi , ukulingana , isidima somntu , ubomi nobulungisa bentlalo . .
Ikharityhulamu izama ukuyila umfundi ofunda ubomi bonke , ozithembileyo , ozimelayo , ofundileyo , okwazi ukubala onobuchule obuninzi , onothando nonentlonipho yommandla nonobuchule bokuthatha inxaxheba kuluntu njengommi ohluzayo nokhutheleyo . .
INTSHAYELELO YENKALO YESIFUNDO YEELWIMI - ISIXHOSA .
INkcazelo .
INkalo yeziFundo yeeLwimi iquka : .
Zonke iilwimi ezilishumi elinanye zaseburhulumenteni isiPedi , isiSuthu , Siswati , isiTswana , Xitsonga , Tshivenda , isiBhulu , isiNgesi isiNdebele , isiXhosa , isiZulu . .
Iilwimi ezivunywe yiBhodi yeeLwimi Zonke zoMzantsi Afrika , iPan South African Board ( PANSALB ) neBhodi eLawula iziQinisekiso zaBafundi beBanga leshumi eline sibini eMzantsi Afrika , iSouth Afrika Certification Boardi ( SAFCERT ) , ezifana nolwimi lweMinwe neBreyile . .
INkalo yesiFundo yolwimi lwaseburhulumenteni nganye yaziswe njengeenxalenye ezintathu iyileyo inomthamo wayo ; ulwimi lwenkobe , ulwimi olongezelelweyo lokuqala , nolwimi olongezelelweyo lwesibini . .
Kwilizwe elineelwimi ezininzi njengeloMzantsi Afrika kubaluleke kakhulu ukuba abafundi bafikelele kumanqanaba aphezulu obuchule beelwimi ezimbini ubuncinane , kwaye bakwazi nokunxibelelana ngezinye iilwimi . .
INkqubo yoNgezelelo kwiiLwimi eziNinzi .
INkalo yesiFundo yeeLwimi ihambisana nomgaqo wolwimi kwimfundo yeSebe leMfundo . .
Lo mgaqo unika amaBhunga aLawula iziKolo uxanduva lokwenza imigaqo yolwimi lwesikolo efanele iimeko zabo kwaye ehambisana nomgaqo wongezelelo kwiilwimi ezininzi . .
INkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo yeelwimi inika ikharityhulamu exhasa nasiphi isigqibo esenziwa sisikolo . .
Ilandela inkqubo yongezelelo kwiilwimi ezininzi .
Bonke abafundi bafunda ulwimi lwabo lwenkobe nolwimi olunye olongezelelweyo ubuncinane . .
Abafundi baba nobuchule kulwimi olongezelelweyo ekubeni ulwimi lwenkobe lulondolozwa kwaye lukwa . .
Bonke abafundi bafunda iilwimi zesiNtu kangangeminyaka emithandathu ekupheleni kwebakala GET . .
Kwezinye iimeko lungafundwa njengolwimi lwesibini olongezelel weyo . .
Ulwimi lwenkobe , iilwimi ezongezelelweyo , elokuqala nelesibini zenziwe ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo : .
Imigangatho yokuhlola yolwimi lwenkobe luqikelela ukuba abafundi beza esikolweni sebeluqonda kwaye beluthetha ulwimi . .
Baxhasa ukukhuliswa kobu buchule , ingakumbi ngokuphathelele kwiintlobo ezahlukeneyo zobuchule ( bokufunda , bokubhala , bokubona nokuhlautya ) . .
Obu buchule bunika ikharityhulamu eyomeleleyo ukuxhasa ulwimi lokufunda nokufundisa ( LOLT ) . .
Ulwimi olongezelweyo lokuqala luqikelela ukuba abafundi abanalwazi lolwimi xa befika esikolweni . .
Ikharityhulamu yesikolo iqalisa ngokukhulisa ubuchule bengqiqo nobokuthetha ulwimi . .
Kwesi siseko lwakha ubuchule . .
Abafundi bayakwazi ukugqithisela ubuchule ababufumene kulwimi lwenkobe kulwimi lokuqala olongezelelweyo . .
Ikharityhulamu inika inkxaso eyomeleleyo kwabo bafundi abaza kuqala ukusebenzisa ulwimi lokuqala olongezelelweyo njengolwimi lokufunda nokufundisa kwezinye iincam zebakala leGET . .
Ekupheleni kweBanga le , aba bafundi kufuneka bakwazi ukusebenzisa ulwimi lwabo lwenkobe nolongozelelweyo ngokufanelekieyo nangokuzithemba kwiinjongo ezahlukeneyo ukuquka nokufunda . .
Ulwimi lwesibini olongezelelweyo lujolise kubafundi abanqwenela ukufunda iilwimi ezintathu . .
Ulwimi lwesithathu lungaba lulwimi olusemthethweni okanye ulwimi lwa mazwe ngamazwe . .
Imigangatho yokuhlola iqinisekisa ukuba abafundi bayakwazi ukusebenzisa ulwimi kwiinjongo zonxibelelwano jikelele . .
Ziqikelela ukuba lixeshana elincinane eliya kwabelwa ukufundwa kolwimi lwesibini olongezelweyo kuneliya kwaba elwa ulwimi lwenkobe nolokuqala olongezelelweyo . .
INkalo yesiFundo yeeLwimi iquka iilwimi ezili zaseburhulumenteni : .
ulwimi lwenkobe .
ulwimi lokuqala olongezelelweyo .
ulwimi lwesibini olongezelelweyo .
ULwimi lokuFunda nelokuFundisa ( LOLT ) .
Sicebisa ukuba ulwimi lwenkobe lomfundi kufuneka lusetyenziswe ekufundeni nasekufundiseni ( LOLT ) apho kuyimfuneko . .
Oku kubaluleke kakhulu kwisiGaba esisiSeko apho abantwana bafunda ukufunda nokubhala . .
Apho abafundi kufuneka beguqukele kulwimi olongezelelweyo ngeenjongo zokufunda nokufundisa ( LOLT ) kufuneka oku kuqulunqwe ngocoselelo : .
Ulwimi olongezelelweyo kufuneka luqaliswe njengesifundo ukufundwa kwangethuba . .
Ulwimi lwenkobe kufuneka luqhutyelwe phambili kangangoko ukusetyenziswa ngethuba kusetyenziswa nolwimi olongezelelweyo . .
Apho abafundi bangena isikolo ulwimi lokufunda nokufundisa ilulwimi olongezelelweyo , ootitshala nesikolo kufuneka banike uncedo nenkxaso yokufunda ulwimi olongezelelweyo kude kube lixesha apho umfundi akwaziyo ukufunda ngokufanelekileyo kulwimi lokufunda nokufundisa ( LOLT ) . .
INjongo .
Iilwimi zikwincam yobomi bethu . .
Sinxibelelana kwaye siqonde ihlabathi ngolwimi . .
Ulwimi ngoko lubumba ubunguwe nolwazi . .
Iilwimi zenza iinjongo ezahlukeneyo , ezibonisiweyo kwiNkcazelo yeNkalo yesifundo yeeLwimi . .
Ezi zezi : .
Ezobuqu - ukugcina ukwalamana okuluqilima kusapho nakuluntu , ukuzazi ubuni bakho , ukuziphuhlisa nokuzonwabisa . .
Unxibelelwano - ukunxibelelana ngokufanelekileyo nangempumelelo kwiimeko zentlalo . .
funda - ukukhulisa izixhobo zokucinga nokuqiqa kwaye kunikwe indlela yokufikelela kulwazi . .
Ubuhle - ukusebenzisana ngomlomo , ngokubonwayo nangoncwadi olubhaliweyo ngokuyila nangokuthelekelela . .
Inkcubeko - ukuqonda nokuxabisa iilwimi neenkcubeko nelifa abanalo . .
politiko - ukuvuma nokucela umngeni kummandla , ukucenga abanye ngoluvo oluthile , ukubeka abanye nokuphuhlisa nokugcina nokuguqula ubungabo . .
Ngokunzulu - ukuqonda ulwalamano phakathi kweelwimi , amandla , nobunguwe , nokucela umngeni ekusetyenzisweni kwezi zinto apho kuyimfuneko . .
Ukuqonda isimo sokuguquguquka kwenkcubeko nokuxhathisa kukucengwa nokubekwa apho kuyimfuneko . .
IimPawu ezizoDwa nomMandla .
Inagalelo lini iNkalo yesiFundo yeeLwimi kwikharityhulamu ? .
iphuhlisa ukufunda nokubhala , okusisiseko sezinye izakhono ezibalulekileyo . .
yindlela yokufunda ezinye izifundo kwikharityhulamu ezinjengemathematika nezenzululwazi yentlalo . .
ikhuthaza ingqiqo yenkcubeko ezahlukeneyo nokufikelela kwiinjongo zabanye nengqiqo enzulu yesigama senkcubeko . .
ivuselela iintelekelelo nesiphiwo sokuyila kwaye ziphucule iinjongo zobugcisa nenkcubeko . .
inika indlela yokunxibelela ulwazi , nokuphucula iinjongo ezininzi zemfundo ngenzululwazi , zeteknoloji , nemfundo yommandla . .
yandisa izixhobo eziyimfuneko zokuba ngabemi abathembekileyo besizwe . .
Iilwimi : ukuhlanganisa ulwazi , ubuchule nokuxabiseka .
Kuneziphumo ezi eziphambili : .
iziphumo ezi zokuqala zibhekiselele kubuchule obu obahlukeneyo bolwimi ( ukumamela , ukuthetha , uku , ukubukela nokubhala . .
isiphumo sesi sibhekiselele ekusebenziseni iilwimi ngeenjongo zokucinga nokuqiqa ezibalulekileyo kulwi lokufunda nokufundisa ( LOLT ) . .
isiphumo sesi sisebenza ngembilini yolwimi izandi , amagama negrama - kwisicatshulwa . .
Olu lwazi luse ngobuchule bolwimi oluchazwe kwezinye iziphumo . .
Ezi ziphumo zibhalwe ngokunika ingqalelo ethile kuhlobo oluthile lolwazi , nobuchule obuthile ukuzenza zicace kwaye ziqondakale . .
Xa sisebenzisa ulwimi sidibanisa ulwazi , ubuchule nokuxabiseka ukuzivakalisa . .
Umgaqo ongundoqo weNgxelo yesiFundo yeeLwimi ngoko kukudityaniswa kwezimo zolwimi ekuyileni nasekutolikeni izicatshulwa . .
IziPhumo zesiFundo zoLwimi .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo soku : UkuMamela .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukumamela ulwazi , kwaye emamelelele nokuzonwabisa aze aphendule ngokufaneleki nangokunzulu kwiimeko ngokubanzi . .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo sesi : UkuThetha .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukunxibelelana ngempumelelo nangokuzithemba , ngolwimi oluthethwayo kwiimeko ezibanzi . .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo sesi : UkuFunda nokubukela .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukufunda nokubukela ulwazi kwaye afundele ukuzonwabisa aze aphendule kubuhle , kwinkcubeko nakukuxabiseka okunovakalelo kwizicatshulwa . .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo sesi : UkuBhala .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukubhala iindidi zezicatshulwa ezahlukeneyo ezineengongoma ezinobunyaniso nezentelekelelo kwiinjongo ezininzi ezibanzi . .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo sesi : UkuCinga nokuQiqa .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukusebenzisa ulwimi ekucingeni nasekuqiqeni , ekwafikelela kulwazi , esetyisa aze alusebenzise ekufundeni . .
IsiPhumo sesiFundo : UkwAkhiwa nokuSetyenziswa koLwimi .
Umfundi uyakwazi ukuqonda kwaye akwazi ukusebenzisa izandi , isigama negrama yolwimi ukuyila nokutolika izicatshulwa . .
Ukuhlanganisa iziphumo .
Ukumamela nokuthetha , ukufunda nokubukela , ukubhala , ukucinga nokuqiqa , nolwazi lwezandi , amagama , negrama kufuneka zidityaniswe xa zifundiswa naxa zihlolwa nangona zinikwe njengeziphumo ezahlukeneyo . .
Umzekelo : Abafundi baya : .
kumamela uhlobo oluthile lwesicatshulwa ( umzekelo , inkcazelo yenkqubo efana nokwembiwa kwegolide okanye ukwenza iphepha ) ; .
kufunda bahlalutye iimpawu eziphambili zesinye isicatshulwa esiluhlobo olufanayo nolu lungentla ( umzekelo : ukusebenzisa ixesha langoku , nezihlanganisi , ezifana kodwa , ukuze , kuba ) ; .
kubhala isicatshulwa esitsha sohlobo olufanayo ukuquka izixhobo ezibonwayo kwisimo somzobo ojikelezayo . .
Ukuyila nokutolika izicatshulwa .
Ukuze abafundi bakwazi ukuyila nokutolika kufuneka babe nolwazi malunga nolwimi , ulwazi , malunga nezicatshulwa , ubuchule neendlela zolwimi .
Izicatshulwa zingaba : .
zezomlomo , umz : intetho .
ezibhalwayo , umz : ileta .
intlanganisela yokubhalwayo nokubonwayo , umzekelo isazisi .
ezezixhobo zokusasaza ezininzi , umz : izicatshulwa zethelevizhini , .
Ulwazi lolwimi nolwezicatshulwa ukuquka nolwazi malunga : .
nemeko - injongo , isihloko nabaphula .
nesakhiwo sesicatshulwa , umz : somhobe , okanye sesazisi .
nolwimi nolunxulumene nemvumelwano noqheliso lwentlalo , umz : indlela abantu ababulisa ngayo kwiilwimi ezahlukeneyo .
negrama , izandi , nesigama solwimi .
nobhalo nopelo lwesicatshulwa esibhaliweyo .
nemifanekiso noyilo kwisicatshulwa esibonwayo .
Ukuhlanganisa ulwimi : ukuxabiseka .
Zonke izicatshulwa ziqulathe ukuxabiseka okwakhayo ( umz : idemokrasi ) okanye okungakhiyo ( isini , ubuhlanga ) . .
Oku kuxabiseka akusoloko kucacile . .
Abafundi kufuneka bakuqaphele oku kwaye bahlalutye ukuxabiseka okukhoyo kwizicatshulwa abazifundayo nabazibukelayo nezo baziyile ngokwabo . .
Xa abafundi behlalutya , apho kuyimfuneko , kwaye becela umngeni ngendlela ekubekwe ngayo ukuxabiseka kwizicatshulwa zomlomo , ezibonwayo nezibhalwayo baya : .
kufunda , ukuba izicatshulwa ziyithatha njani imbono ethile yabantu neziganeko . .
kwandisa ubuchule obunzulu bokuvavanya kwaye ukuba kuyimfuneko bachase ezi mbono nokuxabiseka kwazo okuphathelele kubo . .
kuqaphela indlela yokuvakalisa ukuxabiseka okukwizicatshulwa eziyilwe ngabo umz : unyamezelwano , uvelwano , ulonwabo , ubuhle , uburharha , ukuthanda ukudlala ) kwizicatshulwa ezenziwe ngabo . .
Ukuhlanganiswa kokufundwa kolwimi : imixholo .
Ukufundwa kolwimi lusenokuhlanganiswa ngemixholo . .
Ukusebenzisa umxholo kuvumela umfundi ukuba akhe isigama esiphathelele kwisihloko . .
Ukhetho olululo lwemixholo nezihloko aluniki ntlanganisela kuphela , lukwakhuthaza umdla wabafundi . Ukuphumelelisa oku , kufuneka uzame : .
ukufumana ulungelelwaniso lwezihloko nemixholo ethi inike umdla kumakhwenkwe namantombazana , kubafundi basezidolophini nabasemaphandleni imixholo ethi ihlanganise abafundi kule yantlukwano . .
ukukhetha izihloko ezinxulumene nobomi babafundi , kwaye zibe ngaphaya koko sebekwazi kakade . .
Umz . : bangafunda ngamanye amazwe neenkcubeko . .
nokukhetha imixholo nezihloko ezinxulumana neziphumo ezingundoqo nezakhayo . umzekelo , abafundi kufu bazibandakanye kwimibandela ebalulekileyo yamalungelo oluntu , ommandla efana nobuhlwempu , HIV / AIDS , ilungelo kumhlaba , nolwimi olusetyenziswa ngabathengi . .
Amalungelo oluntu nobulungisa bommandla .
Iilwimi zizixhobo ezibalulekileyo ukuphumelelisa amalungelo oluntu nobulungisa bommandla . .
Ngemigangatho yokuhlola iNkcazelo yeNkalo yesiFundo yeeLwimi izama ukukhulisa esi sixhobo sibe kwawona mandla waso aleleyo . .
Abafundi abanezixhobo ezinzulu zokufunda ngelizwe labo nangezicatshulwa ezithethwayo nezibhalwayo malunga nalo kufuneka bazithembe kwiilwimi ezimbini ( okanye kwiilwimi ezininzi ) . .
Kufuneka bakwazi ukuhlalutya ezi zicatshulwa kwaye baphinde bazibhale ngeendlela ezandisa amathuba onxulumano lwamalungelo oluntu nobulungisa bommandla . .
ISAHLUKO SESI .
UKUHLOLWA KOMFUNDI .
INTSHAYELELO .
Isakhelo sokuhlola seNkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe samaBanga R ukuya kwele isekeke kwimigaqo yenkqubo yemfundo esekeke kwiziphumo . .
UHlolo kufuneka lunike izalathisi zempumelelo yomfundi ngendlela efanelekileyo nokuqinisekisa ukuba abaFundi bahlanganisa kwaye basebenzisa ulwazi nobuchule . .
UHlolo kufu luncede abafundi ekwenzeni izigwebo malunga nokwenziwe ngabo , ukumisa iinjongo zenkqubela nokwenza baqhubele phambili ukufunda . .
Ukuncedisa inkqubo yokuhlola iNkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe : .
Ibonisa iziphumo zesifundo nemigangatho yokuhlola ehambisana nazo kwiNkalo yesiFundo ngasinye nakwibanga ngalinye lemfundo noQeqesho Jikelele ( Amabanga ukusuka kuR ukuya kwibanga lesi ) . .
Ngqamanisa iziPhumo ezinguNdoqo nezoPhuhliso kwiziPhumo zesiFundo nemiGangatho yokuHlola kwiNkalo yesiFundo nganye . .
Beka imiGangatho yokuHlola embindini wenkqubo yokuhlola kwibanga ngalinye . .
Ichaza umgangatho apho abafundi kufuneka bebonise ukuphumelela kwabo iziphumo zezifundo kunye neendlela ( zobunzulu nobubanzi ) zokubonisa ukuphumelela kwabo . .
Lo mzobo ulandelayo ubonisa intsebenziswano phakathi kweempawu zesakhiwo zale Nkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe : .
IMIGAQO YOHLOLO ESETYENZISWA KWIMFUNDO ESEKEKE KWIZIPHUMO .
INkcazelo .
Uhlolo kwiNkcazelo yeKharityhulamu yeSizwe eHlaziyiweyo yamaBanga ukusuka ku ukuya kwele ( ezikolo ) izingile kwaye yinkqubo equlunqelwe ukuqokelela ulwazi malunga nokwenziwa ngumfundi okulinganiswa ngemiGangatho yokuHlola yeziPhumo zeziFundo . .
Lufuna ukuba imilinganiselo yohlolo ichazwe ngokucacileyo kwaye lufuna neendlela ezifanelekileyo ezivumela ootitshala ukuba banike iingxelo eyakhayo kubafundi nokuni ingxelo kubazali , nakwabanye abantu abanomdla . .
IiMpawu ezinguNdoqo .
Imfundo esekeke kwiziphumo yindlela yokufunda nokufundisa eyenza kucace oko kulindelwe kokuba kuphu ngumfundi . .
Umgaqo esebenza ngayo kukuba utitshala uchaza kwantlandlolo ekulindelwe kumfundi . .
Umsebenzi katitshala kukufundisa abafundi ukubanceda ukuba banelise iimfuno zemiGangatho yokuHlola ekwikharityhulamu , uze umsebenzi womfundi ube kukufunda okanye ukwenza oko kulindelwe yimiGangatho yokuHlola . .
Uhlolo luyafuneka kwimfundo esekeke kwiziphumo kuba lwenza kuhlolwe oko kuphunyelelwa ngumfundi okufunekayo kwibanga elilandelayo . .
Ukunceda abafundi ukuba bafikelele kowona mgangatho wabo uphezulu wokwenza izinto ngempumelelo , uhlolo kufuneka : .
lwenziwe ngendlela ecacileyo kwaye lujolise ngokucacileyo .
luhlanganiswe nokufundisa nokufunda . .
lusekwe kwimigangatho okanye kwimilinganiselo esele imiselwe . .
lwahluka ngokuphathelele kwiimethodi , kwaye . .
lunyaniseke , lulunge , luthembeke , lube nobulungisa , luhambe ngokwesantya somfundi . .
INjongo yokuHlola .
Eyona njongo yokuhlolwa kwabafundi engundoqo kufuneka ibe kukukhuliswa nokuphuhliswa kwabo , ukulandela inkqubela yabafundi nokuqhubela phambili ukufunda kwabo . .
Eminye imisebenzi yohlolo iquka : .
uhlolo olusisiseko koko sele kusaziwa .
Uhlolo olusisiseko ludla ngokwenziwa ekuqaleni kwebanga okanye ibakala ukuzinzisa oko sele kusaziwa .
ngabafundi . .
Lunceda utitshala ekuqulunqeni iinkqubo zokufunda nemisebenzi yokufunda . .
uhlolo lwezidingo zomfundi .
Uhlolo lwezidingo zomfundi lusetyenziselwa ukufumana malunga nesimo nesizathu zezithintelo zokufunda .
ezifunyanwa ngumfundi othile . .
Oku kunika ithuba lokuba kunikwe inkxaso efanelekileyo , .
iindlela zokungenelela . .
uhlolo olwakhayo Uhlolo olwakhayo lulawula kwaye luxhasa inkqubo yokufunda nokufundisa kwaye lukwasetyenziswa ekuxele abafundi nootitshala malunga nenkqubela yabafundi ukuphucula ukufunda . .
Ingxelo eyakhayo iyanikwa ukukhulisa umfundi . .
uhlolo olushwankathelayo .
Uhlolo olushwankathelayo lunika umfanekiso wonke wenkqubela yomfundi wexesha elimisiweyo okanye ukuphela konyaka okanye ukugqithiselwa kwesinye isikolo . .
UHLOLO OLUZINGILEYO .
IiMpawu zoHlolo oluZingileyo .
Uhlolo oluzingileyo yindlela engundoqo uhlolo olwenzeka ngayo kwiNkcazelo yeKharityhulamu eHlaziyiweyo . .
Luquka yonke imigaqo yokuhlola yemfundo esekeke kwiziphumo kwaye luqinisekisa ukuba : .
lwenzeka ngaphaya kwexesha kwaye luzingile : Ukufunda kuhlolwa njalo kwaye iingxelo zenkqubela phambili yabafundi ihlaziywa unyaka wonke . .
luxhasa ukukhuliswa nokuphuhliswa kwabafundi : Abafundi baba ngabathathi nxaxheba abakhutheleyo ekufundeni nakuhlolo , kwaye bayayiqonda inqobo esetyenzisiweyo kwimisebenzi yohlolo , bayabandakanyeka ekuzivavanyeni , bazibekela abakwenzayo , baze bahlaziye ukufunda kwabo ngokwenza njalo babe banyusa umgangatho wobuyena . .
lunika ingxelo ekufundeni nasekufundiseni : Ingxelo ngundoqo kuhlolo olwakhayo . .
Iimethodi zengxelo ziquka ukubuza imibuzo ngokufanelekileyo , kwaye zijolise kukuphawula ngomlomo kukatitshala nakokubhaliweyo koko kufuneka kuphunyelelwe ngumsebenzi wohlolo , nokukhuthazwa komfundi . .
luvumela uhlanganiso lohlolo : Oku kungaquka iqela leziPhumo zesiFundo ezinxulumeneyo kumsebenzi owodwa wokuhlola , kwaye kudityaniswe iqela leemethodi zokuhlola ezahlukeneyo , ubuchule , nezixhobo . .
Ubuchule kwiziPhumo zokuHlola zinokuboniswa ngeendlela ezahlukeneyo , kungoko iimethodi zohlolo ezahlukeneyo namathuba kufuneka enikiwe ukuze abafundi babe nokubonisa ubuchule babo . .
lusebenzisa iindlela ezijongene nezidingo zomfundi ezahlukeneyo ( ulwimi , inkangeleko , ubume bengqondo , uvakalelo nenkcubeko ) Uhlolo oluzingileyo luvumela ootitshala ukuba babe novakalelo kubafundi abanezidingo ezithile zemfundo nokwahlula izithintelo ngeenkqubo ezinobumvoco . .
Nakuliphi iqela labafundi kukho izantya ezahlukeneyo nezimbo zokufunda ezahlukeneyo . .
Abafundi abanakuhlolwa bonke ngexesha elinye nangendlela enye . .
luvumela uhlolo olushwankathelayo : Ingqokelela yeziphumo zemisebenzi yohlolo oluzingileyo inika umfanekiso jikelele wenkqubela phambili yomfundi kwixesha elinikiweyo . .
Uhlolo olushwankathelayo kufune luqulunqwe ngononophelo kwasekuqaleni konyaka , ukuquka neendlela ezahlukeneyo zohlolo - umzekelo , imisebenzi , imisetyenzana , iiprojekthi , iimvavanyo zesikolo nezeklasi - eziya kunika abafundi amathuba amaninzi okubonisa oko bakufundileyo . .
IiNdlela ngeeNdlela zokuHlola .
Ukhetho lokusetyenziswa kweendlela zokuhlola zisoloko ziqhutywa luluvo , kwaye zahluka ngokwetitshala nganye , ngokwebanga nangokwesikolo kwaye luxhomekeke kubuchule bokugweba bukatitshala . .
Ukubakho kwendawo nobutyebi bunempembelelo kwesi sigqibo , kodwa xa ubutyebi bufana , ootitshala bahlukana ngeendlela abenza ngazo ukhetho . .
Iimethodi ezikhethelwe imisebenzi yohlolo kufuneka zifanele imiGangatho yokuHlola ehlolwayo , kwaye injongo yohlolo kufuneka iqondwe ngokucacileyo ngabafundi bonke kwanootitshala ababandakanyekayo . .
Ubuchule bungaboniswa ngeendlela eziliqela . .
Iimethodi ezahlukeneyo ngoko ziyimfuneko ekunikeni abafundi ithuba lokubonisa ubuchule babo ngokupheleleyo . .
UmSebenzi wokuHlola oFanayo .
Injongo yomsebenzi wohlolo ofanayo kuku : .
qinisekisa ukungaguquguquki kwezigwebo zikatitshala ; .
phucula umgangatho wokuseta ofanayo ; .
nika amandla kumthamo wohlolo oluzingileyo olusekeke esikolweni ; .
andisa ukufaneleka kwenkqubo nezixhobo zohlolo ; .
qinisekisa ukuba imisebenzi yohlolo olusekeke esikolweni luhlola ubuchule ; .
nempumelelo ngokufanelekileyo ; .
nokuqinisekisa ukwandisa amathuba abafundi . .
Imisebenzi yohlolo efanayo ingamiselwa kwinqanaba isizwe lephondo lenqila okanye lezikolo ezihlangeneyo . .
Oku kungenziwa kwinqanaba lesikolo kwaye lubekwe emgangathweni ngabantu bangaphandle . .
UKULAWULWA KOHLOLO .
AbaNtu abaBandakanyeka kuHlolo .
Isikolo nootitshala banoxanduva jikelele lokuhlola abafundi . .
Ootitshala balindeleke ukuba bayile inkqubo yohlolo enyanisekileyo , ethembekileyo kwaye ekholelekayo . .
Imigaqo yamaphondo kufuneka iqinisekise ukubandakanywa kwabafundi , amaqela ohlolo esikolo , amaqela enqila axhasayo , iinkonzo zenkxaso , abazali ngokufanelekileyo . .
inkqubo yesikolo yohlolo .
Isikolo ngasinye kufuneka sivelise umgaqo wohlolo osekeke kwizikhokelo zokuhlola zephondo nezesizwe . .
Kufuneka sibe neQela loYilo lokuHlola lesiKolo ukuqhubela phambili ukuzalisekiswa kwenkqubo . .
Eli qela kufu limelwe sisigaba ngasinye nayiNkalo yesiFundo nganye . .
Ukuqinisekisa inkqubo enobuchule kuhlolo , umgaqo wohlolo wesikolo kufuneka ucacise ngokucacileyo : .
indlela uhlolo oluzingileyo oluqulunqwa ngayo noluzalisekiswa ngayo ; .
indlela iincwadi zengxelo ezigcinwa ngayo , ukufikelela nokhuseleko ; .
iikhowudi zohlolo ezimiselwe liphondo ; .
isiqinisekiso sangaphakathi sesikolo ; .
indlela yokubeka emgangathweni okwenziwayo esikolweni ; .
indlela esetyenziswa njalo yokunika ingxelo ; .
ukujonga zonke iinkqubo zohlolo ; .
nokuqeqeshwa kwestafu kwiinkalo zohlolo . .
Iinkalo apho iimfuno zoqeqesho lwesikolo kufuneka zenziwe ziquka : .
indlela yokusetyenziswa komlinganiselo / indlela yolawulo yokuhlolwayo ekuhloleni ; .
ukufumana imvumelwano phakathi kweetitshala zebanga elinye ngokufuneka kwenziwe ukwanelisa iziPhumo zesiFundo ; .
indlela yokubhala amagqabantshintshi emisebenzi yokuhlola neengxelo ; .
nokuphumelela kwengqiqo efanayo yenkqubo yohlolo yesikolo . .
UKUGCINWA KWENGXELO .
IiNcwadi zeNgxelo .
Ukugcinwa kwengxelo okulungileyo kubalulekile kulo lonke uhlolo ingakumbi kuhlolo oluzingileyo . .
Incwadi yengxelo okanye ifayile kufuneka igcinwe ngutitshala . .
Le ncwadi iqulathe : .
amagama abafundi ; .
imihla yokuhlola ; .
igama nenkcazelo yomsebenzi wohlolo ; .
iziphumo zemisebenzi yohlolo ngokweNkalo yesiFundo neNkqubo yokuFunda ; .
namagqabantshintshi ngeenjongo zokuxhaswa . .
Zonke iingxelo kufuneka zifikeleleke , zitolikeke ngokulula , zigcinwe ngokukhuselekileyo , njengehlebo , kwaye zibe luncedo kwinkqubo yokufundisa nokunika ingxelo . .
INkqubo yohlolo yesikolo imisela iinkcukacha zeendlela zokugcwaliswa kweencwadi zengxelo . .
Iikhowudi zohlolo ezikhethiweyo zisetyenziselwa ukuvakalisa indlela umfundi enza ngayo ngokweziPhumo zesiFundo . .
Iikhowudi ezisetyenziswayo kufuneka zicacile kwaye ziqondwe ngabafundi nabazali . .
IiKhowudi eziSetyenziswa kuHlolo .
Kuneendlela ezininzi zokunika iingxelo kubafundi ngohlolo nokugcinwa ngootitshala . .
Ukukhetha eyona ndlela elungileyo yokwenza oku umsebenzi wohlolo uxhomekeka kwiqela leemeko ezifana : .
neqela labafundi eklasini nobungakanani bexesha analo utitshala ; .
nokuntsonkotha nobude bomsebenzi wohlolo ; .
nomxholo ofundiweyo okanye ubuchule obuhlolwayo ( iMathematika okanye ubhalo ) ; .
nokuba ingxelo inikwa ngokukhawuleza kangakanani ; .
nokuba ingxelo ngabanye ngabanye yenziwa njani ; .
nomlinganiselo ( indlela esetyenziswa ekuhloleni ) osetyenziswa ngutitshala ukuchaza okwenziwa ngumfundi ; .
nokuba okwenziwa ngumfundi kuthelekiswa nabalingane , nokwenziwe kwixesha elidlulileyo , kunye / okanye iimfuno zemiGangatho yokuHlola neziPhumo zesiFundo . .
Ezinye iikhowudi zohlolo zingcono kunezinye . .
Umzekelo , amagqabantshintshi anganzulu , kwaye anike iingce zophuculo . .
Amagqabantshintshi aluncedo ekunikeni ingxelo ngokwenziwa ngabafundi ngokwemiGangatho yokuHlola . .
Nangona kunjalo , amagqabantshintshi athatha ixesha elide ukubhalwa kwaye akukho lula ukuwarekhodisha . .
Iikhowudi ezifana ugqithisile , kulunge kakhulu , kulungile , unobuchule akwanelisanga kulula ukuzibhala kwaye zivumela uhlolo lwenkqubela phambili ngokomsebenzi odlulileyo nangokwemiGangatho yokuHlola . .
Nangona kunjalo , aziniki bunzulu obenziwa ngokulindelwe ngamagqabantshintshi . .
Amanqaku kwelinye icala arekhodisheka lula kwaye angadityaniswa , aphinda kwaye ahlula . .
Aluncedo ekuhloleni okwenziwa ngabafundi ngokunxulumene kwabanye eklasini , nakwamanye amabanga okanye esikolweni . .
Nangona kunjalo anika ulwazi oluncinane ngokwenziwa ngabafundi ngokwemiGangatho yokuHlola . .
Imizekelo phakathi kweminye emininzi yeekhowudi zohlolo zokuqhubela phambili : .
akakaphumeleli , usondele , uphumelele ; .
okwenziwayo kuyanelisa , kufuna inkxaso ; .
A , B , C ; .
namabinza enzelwe umsebenzi ohlolwayo okanye ingxelo . .
Nokokuba yiyiphi ikhowudi yohlolo esetyenziswayo , ingxelo inentsingiselo xa ikhatshwa ngamagqabantshintshi . .
Kungakho uphuculo kokuphunyelelweyo xa abafundi benikwe ingxelo ebhaliweyo kunokunikwa amanqaku kuphela . .
Nangona amanqaku neepesenti ziluncedo kakhulu njengoko kulula ukubhala amanqaku kwincwadi yengxelo , awaloncedo ekunikeni ingxelo . .
Ezinye iingxaki ezenziwa ngamanqaku angandiswa kwaye angasetyenziselwa ezinye iinjongo kwaye afihla okuninzi ngokuphunyelelwe ngumfundi nenkqubela phambili . .
Ukuba umfundi ugqibe ngaphezulu komsebenzi omnye ohlolwayo kuya kubakho umtsalane wokusebenzisa amanqaku , ukudibanisa nokubeka kumgangatho othile . .
Xa oku kusenziwa amanqaku awaloncedo ekunikeni ulwazi . .
Umgangatho ufihla okubekunokuphunyelelwa ngokulungileyo ngumfundi kukufunda ebekulindelwe kwisimo esithile kunakwesinye . .
Amanqaku anika imbonakalo jikelele yokuphunyelelwayo aze afihle izizathu zoku kohlolo ( okanye ukunqongophala kokuphunyelelweyo ) ngumfundi kwaye kuthintela ugqaliselo ekufundeni okuthile kuhlolo . .
Kwaye akachazi inkqubela phambili yomfundi kwikharityhulamu . .
Kumaxesha amaninzi ukugcina inqaku elifanayo ( ngaphandle kokuba luyanelisa ) luthathwa njengesalathisi esanelisayo senkqubela phambili . .
Amanqaku angama ngokwemiGangatho yokuHlola yeBanga lesi namanqaku angama ngokwemiGangatho yokuHlola yeBanga lesi ayifihla ngokupheleleyo inkqubela phambili yomfundi angayenza ekuhambeni konyaka , echazwa ngcono kwingxelo , kwikhowudi , okanye kumagqabantshintshi . .
IiKhowudi zeSizwe .
Ekunikeni ingxelo ngempumelelo yomfundi kwiziPhumo zesiFundo zebanga elithile , ezi khowudi zingasetyenziswa : .
4 = Okwenziwe ngumfundi kugqithisile kwimfuno zesiPhumo sesiFundo sebanga .
3 = Okwenziwa ngumfundi kwanelisile kwimfuno zesiPhumo zesiFundo sebanga .
2 = Okwenziwa ngumfundi kunxalenye kwimfuno zesiPhumo zesiFundo sebanga .
1 = Okwenziwa ngumfundi akwanelisanga kwimfuno zesiPhumo zesiFundo sebanga .
UluDwe lweNkqubela .
Ekupheleni konyaka uludwe lwenkqubela kufuneka ibe igqityiwe , ityikitywe yinqununu okanye umsebenzi karhulumente . .
Uludwe lwenkqubela yingxelo enesishwankathelo solwazi malunga nenkqubela yabafundi bonke bebanga esikolweni . .
Uludwe lwenkqubela kufuneka luquke olu lwazi : .
igama lesikolo nesitampu saso ; .
uluhlu lwabafundi kwibanga ngalinye ; .
iikhowudi zenkqubela kwiNkalo yesiFundo nganye ( isixokelelwano seekhowudi zesizwe ) ; .
iikhowudi zenkqubela kwibanga ngalinye ( ukuqhubela phambili ukuya ; kwelinye ibanga okanye ukuhlala kwelo banga umfundi ebekulo ) ; .
phawula kummandla nakwindawo ezifuna inkxaso kwiNkalo yesiFundo nganye ; .
nomhla notyikityo lwenqununu , utitshala nomsebenzi waseburhulumenteni . .
IiNgxelo zomFundi .
Ingxelo yomfundi yingxelo ezingileyo yolwazi jikelele ngembonakalo yenkqubela yomfundi ukuquka uphuhliso olupheleleyo lokuxabiseka , iimbono , nophuhliso lwentlalo . .
Inceda utitshala kwibanga elilandelayo okanye isikolo ukuba azi umfundi ngcono aze aphendule kuye ngokufanelekileyo . .
Ingxelo yomfundi ngamnye kufuneka ikhusele umfundi ngamnye kwaye imkhaphe umfundi kuyo yonke inkqubela yesikolo . .
Olu luhlobo lolwazi kufuneka lubandakanywe kwingxelo yomfundi : .
ulwazi oluphathelele kumfundi ngokunokwakhe ; .
inkangeleko akuyo ngokwempilo kunye nolwazi okanye imbali ngempilo yakhe ; .
izikolo athe wafunda kuzo nerekhodi ebonisa oko ; .
ukuthatha inxaxheba nezinto athe waziphumelela kwizinto ezizezinye ezenziwayo esikolweni ngaphandle kwemfundo ; .
uvakalelo nokuziphatha ; .
ukubandakanyeka kwabazali ; .
indawo apho umfundi asafuna khona uncedo ; .
ingxelo eshwankathelayo equka konke okuthe kwenziwa kulo nyaka ; .
iirekhodi ezishwankathelayo zeminyaka yokufunda ; .
Qaphela : .
Ingxelo yomfundi ithatha indawo yazo zonke iincwadi zokurekhodisha ebezisetyenziswa ngaphambili sisikolo , ezifana namacwecwe okurekhodisha , amacwecwe anenkcazelo abhalwe ngumncedi katitshala , namacwecwe e . .
Injongo engundoqo yengxelo yomfundi kukunceda umfundi ukuba afumane ulwazi olwahluka oluqulethwe kuyo . .
Ulwazi ngaye olukwingxelo akufuneki nanini na ukuba lusetyenziselwe ukucalu ngokungenabulungisa . .
Iingxelo zomfundi kufuneka zingaphazanyiswa nepotifoliyo . .
Ipotifoliyo yindlela yohlolo olunika umfundi notitshala ithuba lokucinga ngomsebenzi omawenziwe kwiqela lemisebenzi yohlolo . .
Umsebenzi ufakwa ebhokisini okanye kwifayile . .
Ingxelo yomfundi ngamanye amazwi yirekhodi equlathe ulwazi ngomfundi . .
IINGXELO .
UlwAzi oluFuneka luBandakanywe kwiiNgxelo .
Utitshala kufuneka aphendule kubafundi , kubazali , kwisixokelelwano semfundo , nakuluntu ngokubanzi ngokuhlolwa komfundi . .
Ukongeza kwiingxelo ezibhalwayo , ukwazisa ngomlomo okanye ngokwenza , imiboniso yemisebenzi yabafundi kungasetyenziswa . .
Ingxelo nganye kwinkqubela phambili yomfundi kufuneka ibandakanye ulwazi : .
ngesifundo esithe saphunyelelwa ; .
ubuchule agqwesa kubo umfundi ; .
uncedo asalufunayo ; .
nengxelo eyakhayo ngoko bekwenziwe ekufuneka kuquke amagqabantshintshi malunga nokwenziwa ngumfundi ngokunxulumene nabalingane nokwenziwe ngumfundi kwixesha elidlulileyo ngokunxulumene neemfuno zeeNkalo zeziFundo . .
Ukunika ingxelo kubazali kufuneka kwenziwe rhoqo ukukhuthaza ukuthathwa kwenxaxheba nokubandakanya abazali kwimfundo yabantwana babo . .
Kuqhelekile ukuba ungabi nako ukunika ulwazi kokuphunyelelwe kwisiPhumo sesiFundo ngasinye . .
Nangona kunjalo iingxelo kufuneka zinike ulwazi ngokuphunyelelweyo kwiNkalo yesiFundo okanye iNkqubo yokuFunda nganye kwimeko yesiGaba esisiseko . .
AmaCwecwe eNgxelo .
Ubuncinane beemfuno zecwecwe lengxelo zi : .
1 ) Ulwazi olusisiseko .
Igama lesikolo ; .
Igama lomfundi ; .
Ibanga akulo umfundi ; .
Unyaka wokuzalwa womfundi ; .
Unyaka nexesha elimisiweyo ; .
Isityikityo sesivumelwano nomhla , esenziwa ngumzali okanye umondli ojongene nemfundo yomfundi . .
Isityikityo sesivumelwano kunye nomhla , esenziwa ngutitshala ; .
Umhla wokuvalwa nalowo wokuvulwa kwezikolo ; .
Isitampu sesikolo ; .
Ingxelo yokuhanjwa kwesikolo ; .
Nokuchazwa kwenkqubo yesizwe yokukhowuda , esetyenzisiweyo . .
2 ) . Amandla nezidingo .
Nika inkcazelo yamandla , izidingo zophuhliso nezo ndawo asafuna uncedo kuzo umfundi kwinkalo yesifundo okanye inkqubo yesifundo nganye . .
Sebenzisa isixokelelwano sokukhowuda sesizwe ukuhlola okwenziwa ngabafundi kwiziPhumo zesiFundo esele zenziwe ngokwemigangatho yokuHlola apho unika ikhowudi ngeNkalo yesiFundo nganye . .
Kwingxelo yokuphela konyaka , bonisa konke okuquka indlela aqhube ngayo umfundi kuzo zonke iziPhumo zesiFundo . .
3 ) Ukwenziwa kwamagqabantshintshi kwiNkalo yesiFundo okanye kwiNkqubo yesiFundo nganye .
Yenza amagqabantshintshi kwinkqubo okanye inkalo yesifundo nganye , ugxininisa kubafundi abenze kakuhle bada bagqithisa kwiimfuno ebezilindelekile okanye abo basafuna uncedo kwiindawo ezithile . .
Nxulumanisa amagqabantshintshi owenzileyo kummandla okanye iindawo umfundi asafuna uncedo kuzo kwimiGangatho yokuHlola . .
La magqabantshintshi aya kunika ithuba abazali , abafundi nabanye abafundisi lokuqonda ukuba luluphi uncedo umfundi aludingayo . .
Kudingeka iphepha lemvume ( ipemethe ) yokungenisa izilwanyana xa ungenisa izilwanyana okanye iimveliso zezilwanyana Riphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Zikho izivumelwano zokungenisa izilwanyana kunye neemveliso zezilwanyana kweli lizwe . .
Njengoko izinto eziyimfuneko zempilo ziguquka rhoqo , nceda unxulumane neCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana ukuze uqonde ngezinto eziyimfuneko zakutshanje . .
Gcwalisa ifom yesicelo . .
Nxulumana neCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana ukuba ngaba akuqinisekanga ukuba ugcwalise eyiphina ifom . .
Faka imali yentlawulo yepemethe kwi yebhanki yeSebe : .
Igama lebhanki .
Igama lomnini .
Inombolo yeakhawunt .
Isebe .
Igama lesebe .
Isaziso esibalulekileyo : Ireferensi kufuneka kube ligama nefani yomngenisi elizweni .
Nceda uqaphele : Umngenisi elizweni unoxanduva leentlawulo zebhanki kwakunye neentlawulo zeBhani yeZizwe iSebe alinakukhupha imvume xa intlawulo epheleleyo ye ingamkelwanga . .
Itshekhi ehlawulwa ku : Agriculture , ingaqhotyoshelwa kwifomu yesicelo ize iposelwe kwidilesi engentla . .
Iintlawulo zingenziwa kananjalo kwiiofisi zeSebe lezoLimo ezikuluhlu lwee zoqhagamshelwano . .
Ukuba wenzela omnye umntu isicelo , nceda uqinisekise ukuba uhlawula phantsi kwegama laloo mntu okanye laloo nkampani . .
Akukho sicelo siyakuphunyezwa ngaphandle kobungqina bentlawulo . .
Ubungqina bentlawulo efakiweyo mabuthunyelwe kwifeksi ethi : 012 329 8292 eyamkelwa ngu : Ina Labuschagne . .
Thumela iifom kule adresi : .

okanye uzithumele kwifeksi ethi 012 329 8292 .
Nceda uchaze kwifom yesicelo ukuba ipemethe izayokuthathwa na okanye kufuneka ithunyelwe kuwe . .
Kwiimeko apho izilwanyana kufuneka zivalelwe , umntu ozingenisa kweli makanxulumane neGosa lokuValelwa kwezilwanyana kwisango lokungena . .
Johannesburg Ifowuni : 011 973 2827 okanye Ifeksi : 011 973 2828 .
Cape Town Ifowuni : 021 551 2050 okanye Ifeksi : 021 551 1378 .
Isikhululo sokuvalela esise Durban asisebenzi okwangoku , kodwa inkcazelo ingafunyanwa kuloo ofisi kwinombolo yomnxeba ethi : 031 368 6011 okanye ngefeksi ethi : 031 337 7469 .
IGosa lokuValela liyakwenza amalungiselelo okubekwa kwendawo kwiSikhululo sokuValela kwaye kufuneka ligcwalise le nxenye ibandakanyekayo yefom yesicelo . .
Iya kuthi ke ifom iphindiselwe ngefeksi kwi yeepemethe , kwaye ke ipemethe yokungenisa kweli lizwe ebandakanyekayo iyakukhutshwa . .
Kufuneka kugcwaliswe ifom yeSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala ( ngokuphathelelene nezilwanyana okanye iintaka ezivalelweyo ezingeniswa kweli lizwe ) kwaye sifakwe apha kwifom yesicelo . .
Le fom yeSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala ingafumaneka nakwi yeePemethe . .
Emva kokufunyanwa kwefom yesicelo egcwalisiweyo , kuyakukhutshwa iPemethe yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli kunye neSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana , zize ke zithunyelwe nqo kuwe . .
Kufuneka kugcwaliswe nge , ngugqirha wezilwanyana ogunyaziselwe ukwenza njalo liZiko loLawulo lwemibandela yeZilwanyana lelizwe elithumela ngaphandle , kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 10 zokumka kwazo . .
Ukuba kukho inkcazelo edingekayo malunga neemfuneko nqo zesilwanyana esithile okanye imveliso ethile yesilwanyana , iikopi zokubonisa zePemethe yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli kunye nezeSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana , zingafumaneka kwi yeePemethe . .
Kufuneka kuvezwe ezi zinto zilandelayo kwiGosa eliLawula ukuNgeniswa kweZilwanyana eMzantsi Afrika kwiSango lokuNgena : .
iPemethe eluqobo lwayo yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli .
iSatifiketi esiluqobo lwaso seMpilo yeZilwanyana .
nayiphina enye incwadi echaziweyo , umzekelo , iSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala , iSatifiketi sokuGonyelwa uMgada , njalo . .
Xa kungeniswa izikhumba namafele kunye neendebe ezimanzi okanye ezomileyo , ifom yesicelo mayingqinwe ngugqirha wombuso kummandla elikuwo eli ziko livunyiweyo . .
Ifom yesicelo mayiphinde ityikitywe kwaye igximfizwe isitampu ngugqirha wombuso obandakanyekayo , oyakuthi yena asibuyisele ngefeksi kwi yeepemethe . .
I yeepemethe iyakukhupha ipemethe yokungenisa izilwanyana kuphela yakube ifumene le fom yesicelo iloluhlobo . .
Xa ungenisa izilwanyana eziphilileyo zasefama , ezifana neenkomo , iigusha , iibhokhwe , amahashe ( ingezizo iikati nezinja ) , kufuneka ufumane ipemethe yokuphucula izilwanyana phambi kokuba kukhutshwe ipemethe yokungenisa izilwanyana . .
Zombini ezi pemethe ziluqobo lwazo kufuneka zithiwe thaca kwiGosa leZilwanyana kwisango lokungena , ndawonye neSatifiketi esiluqobo lwaso seMpilo yeZilwanyana esikhutshwe lilizwe elithumela ngaphandle . .
Amayeza ezilwanyana angangeniswa kwaye athuthelwe kwiindawo ezithile okanye athengiswe eMzantsi Afrika kuphela xa ebhalisiwe ngokoMthetho weZichumiso ( weeFetelayisi ) , uKutya kweMfuyo yaseFama , uNcedo kweZolimo kunye noNcedo kwiMfuyo , lwango 1947 . .
Ukuze ungenise iyeza lokutofa elibhalisiweyo ukuze ulisebenzise kwizilwanyana , kufuneka ufumane iphepha lemvume ( ipemethe ) yokungenisa kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana . .
Le pemethe yokungenisa isebenza ixesha eliqingqiweyo kwaye isebenza kumthwalo omnye kuphela . .
Ukubangaba ufuna ukungenisa iyeza elingabhaliswanga ukuze lilingwe eMzantsi Afrika , kufuneka ubeneepemethe ezimbini . .
Ipemethe yokuqala iphuma kuMphathi woBhaliso ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947 kwaye enye iphuma kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana . .
Isicelo sepemethe ephuma kuMphathi woBhaliso ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947 kufuneka sikhatshwe sisivumelwano esipheleleyo solu lingo lupoposhwayo . .
ICandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana likhupha ipemethe yokungenisa kuphela xa lifumene ikopi yepemethe ekhutshwe nguMphathi woBhaliso ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947 . .
Iyeza elingeniselwe ukulingwa alithengiswa . .
Kwimeko yonxunguphalo , apho kuqhambuke isifo kwaye kungekho yeza libhalisiweyo elifumanekayo eMzantsi Afrika , kungayimfuneko ukuba kusetyenziswe iyeza elingabhaliswanga . .
Ngoko ke , wena , njengomntu onqwenela ukungenisa iyeza kweli lizwe , kufuneka wenze isicelo kwiBhunga lokuLawula aMayeza ukuze ufumane umnyinyiva weCandelo 21 ngokoMthetho woLawulo lwaMayeza neeMveliso ezaYamene nawo ( uMthetho 101 ka 1965 , njengoko ulungisiwe nguMthetho 90 ka 1997 ) . .
Ukwadinga ipemethe yokungenisa , kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana , ukuze eli yeza lingene kweli lizwe . .
Eli Candelo likhupha le pemethe yokungenisa kuphela wakuba ufumene imvume kwiBhunga lokuLawula aMayeza yaye ubuthumele ubungqina kweli candelo . .
Kule meko ke , eli yeza lingabhaliswanga lingathengiswa ixesha eliqingqiweyo kude kufunyanwe ubhaliso . .
Ukubangaba iyeza alibhaliswanga kwaye lizakusetyenziswa kulingo , thumela incwadi yangaphezulu esayiniweyo ebhalelwe kwiphepha elikwisihloko esivunyiweyo senkampani yakho , kuMphathi woBhaliso ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947 , ucele ipemethe yokungenisa . .
Incwadi yakho mayibeneenkcukacha zale miba ilandelyo : .
ubungakanani bomthamo .
igama lemveliso .
isithako okanye izithako ezisebenzayo , kubandakanywa nentlanganisela yezithako .
ilizwe eliphuma kulo .
umenzi weyeza .
inombolo yombhumbutho womthwalo oyakungeniswa .
iphepha lenkcazelo yobuchule okanye umbhalo wokuphawula okuqulathiweyo ( nge ) , onenombolo yobhaliso yequmrhu lokugqalisela lelizwe ebhaliswe kulo le mveliso .
isango lokungena .
inkcazelo yokuba ifuneka nini na le mveliso .
umba wokuba le mveliso ingeniselwa iinjongo zokulingelwa ubhaliso lweemveliso zokunceda imfuyo .
ubume bobhaliso lwemveliso kwezinye iindawo ( oko kukuthi , apho ibhaliswe khona ) .
iSivumelwano soLingo esineenkcukacha ( ngokweemfuno ze GCP ) , kubandakanywa imihla ekulindeleke ukuqaliswa ngayo uqwalaselo olulodwa lekamva lokutya okuphuma kwizilwanyana ezivelisa ukutya ( umzekelo , iyakulahlwa ) kunye nokuthabatha uxanduva lokulandela iimfuno zamachiza . .
Kufuneka ubenephepha lemvume ( ubenepemethe ) yokungenisa izilwanyana xa ungenisa okanye ugqithisa iimveliso zederi eMzantsi Afrika . .
pemithi zokungenisa iimveliso kweli lizwe zisebenza ixesha eliqingqiweyo yaye ziqingqelwa umthwalo omnye kuphela .
Yenza isicelo sepemethe okungenani kwiiveki ezintandathu kodwa ingezoveki ezigqithe isibhozo phambi kokuba uqalise ngamanyathelo eenjongo zakho . .
Gcwalisa ifom yesicelo . .
Ukubangaba le mveliso igqitha apha kwiRiphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika , ikopi yepemethe yokungenisa ephuma kwilizwe eyakuphelela kulo le mveliso mayithiwe thaca kunye nesicelo sepemethe yokugqitha kwezilwanyana yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Faka imali yentlawulo yepemethe kwi yebhanki yeSebe leZolimo : .
Nceda uqaphele : Iintlawulo zebhanki , ndawonye nezeBhanki yaNgaphandle , ziluxanduva lwalo mntu ungenisa imveliso kwe liSebe alisoze likhuphe ipemethe ukuba ngaba intlawulo epheleleyo eyi ayifunyenwanga . .
Ungafaka apha kwifom , itshekhi ebhalelwe ukuhlawuleka kuMqondisi weZolimo , kwaye uyiposele kwi enikiweyo ethubeni . .
Iintlawulo ungazenza nakwii zeSebe leZolimo ezidweliswe phantsi kwesihloko esithi Iinkcukacha zonxulumano . .
Ukuba wenzela omnye umntu isicelo , nceda uqinisekise ukuba uhlawula phantsi kwegama laloo mntu okanye laloo nkampani . .
Akukho sicelo siyakuphunyezwa bungekho ubungqina bentlawulo . .
Ubungqina bokufakwa kwemali bungathunyelwa ngefeksi kwinombolo ethi : 012 329 8292 , bubhalelwe ukwamkelwa ngu : Ina Labuschagne . .
Thumela iifom ezigcwalisiweyo kwi ethi : .
Pretoria .
0001 .
okanye kwi ethi : 012 329 8292 .
Chaza apha kwifom yesicelo ukuba ipemethe uzakuyoyithatha na okanye kufuneka ithunyelwe kuwe . .
Qala uqonde e yeepemethe ngomnxeba ukuba seyilungile na ipemethe phambi kokuba uyokuyithatha . .
Xa sele siyifumene ifom yesicelo egcwalisiweyo , siyakukhupha iPemethe yokuNgeniswa kweZilwanyana kwaye siyithumele kuwe nqo , kunye neSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana , esingumzekelo wokubonisa . .
Esi Satifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana kufuneka sigcwaliswe nge , ngugqirha wezilwanyana ogunyaziselwe ukwenza njalo liZiko loLawulo lwemibandela yeZilwanyana lelizwe elithumela ngaphandle , kwaye siprintwe kwiphepha leli ziko elinesihloko esigunyazisiweyo zingadlulanga iintsuku ezilishumi phambi kokuhanjiswa kwale mveliso . .
Ukuba kukho inkcazelo oyidingayo malunga neemfuneko nqo zemveliso ethile , iikopi zokubonisa zePemethe yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli kunye nezeSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana , zingafumaneka kwi yeePemethe . .
Kufuneka kuvezwe ezi zinto zilandelayo kwiGosa eliLawula ukungeniswa kweZilwanyana eMzantsi Afrika kwiSango lokuNgena : .
iPemethe eluqobo lwayo yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli .
iSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana esiluqobo lwaso esikhutshwe ngugqirha wezilwanyana welizwe ezivela kulo . .
Iimveliso zederi mazihlolwe kwelinye lala maziko okuhlola alandelayo : .
Cape Town : Ifowuni : 021 551 2050 .
City Deep Abattoir ( ephuma kumazwe angabamelwane kuphela ) IFowuni : 011 613 1636 .
Port Elizabeth ( ngemvume eyodwa ) IFowuni : 041 585 8907 .
Izinto eziyimfuneko xa kungeniswa iimveliso kweli lizwe ziyafumaneka kwi yeePemethe okanye kwi yeSebe leZolimo . .
Njengelungu lelabhoratri elinoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa ( inombolo yoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa ithi ZADL01 ) le leHlabathi lokuVavanya iMbewu , ekuthiwa yi Seed Testing Association ( ISTA ) , iSikhululo esiGunyazisiweyo sokuVavanya iMbewu esibizwa ngokuba yi Seed Testing Station ( OSTS ) seSebe leZolimo sigunyazisiwe ukuba sikhuphe iZatifiketi zeHlabathi zokuCazulula iMbewu . .
Ezi zatifiketi zikhutshwelwa iinjongo zokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle . .
Kungakhutshwa iindidi ezintathu zezatifikethi , ezizezi : iZatifiketi zoMthwalo weMbewu ( ziiorenji naluhlaza ) kunye neSatifiketi seBinza ( Sampuli ) leMbewu ( siblowu ) . .
ISatifiketi esi sikhutshwa xa ibinza likhiwe ngokugunyazisiweyo kumthwalo wembewu kwaye uvavanyo luqhutywa phantsi kwegunya lalaa labhoratri inoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa ekhuphe ibinza . .
ISatifiketi esiLuhlaza sikhutshwa xa ibinza likhiwe ngokugunyazisiweyo kumthwalo wembewu phantsi kwegunya lelabhorathri enoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa , kodwa uvavanyo luqhutywa kwenye ilabhorathri enoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa kwelinye ilizwe . .
ISatifiketi esiBlu sikhutshwa xa ukwakhiwa kwebinza kungekho phantsi koxanduva lwelabhoratri enoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa kwaye ilabhorathri enoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa inoxanduva lokuvavanya ibinza kuphela . .
IZatifikethi ezi neziLuhlaza zisebenziseka kumthwalo wembewu ezithathwe kuwo , kodwa sona iSatifiketi esiBlu sisebenziseka kuphela kwibinza elifunyanelwe ukuvavanya . .
Khupha ifom yesicelo seSatifikethi seHlabathi esi kwi uze usigcwalise . .
Njengoko ilabhorathri enoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa kwilizwe elahlukileyo iyakukhupha iSatifiketi eSiluhlaza , nceda unxulumane ne ( jonga iinkcukacha zonxulumano ) . .
Cela ukunikwa amanani agunyazisiweyo emithwalo yembewu . .
Thumela izicelo ngefeksi kwi ( jonga iinkcukacha zonxulumano ) . .
Amanani emithwalo yembewu ayakunikwa kwaye isicelo siyakuphindiselwa kuwe ngefeksi . .
Iya kuthunyelwa ngefeksi nakwigosa eligunyazisiweyo lokuphengulula ( umkhuphi webinza ) kwii zengingqi eziyakukha ibinza . .
Lungisa imithwalo yembewu ukuze kukhiwe amabinza . .
Oku kubandakanya ukuphawula imithwalo ngamanani anikiweyo emithwalo . .
Inkonkxa nganye kufuneka iphawulwe ( ifundeke ngokucacileyo ) okanye incanyatheliswe iphetshana ekubhalwe kulo okuqulathiweyo nelichaza amanani anikiweyo embewu . .
Xa imithwalo yembewu ilungele ukwakhiwa kwamabinza , biza umphengululi azokukha ibinza . .
Amabinza athunyelwa kwi kwaye avavanyelwa umgangatho , kuze ke kukhutshwe isatifiketi esibandakanyekayo . .
Hlawula umlinganiselo wentlawulo yokuvavanya imbewu . .
Kwakube kufunyenwe amabinza , kukhutshwa i . .
Nazi iinkcukacha zebhanki : .
Umhlaba wombuso ( umhlaba ophantsi kolawulo lweSebe lezeMihlaba okanye iSebe lezeMisebenzi yoLwakhiwo kwiindawo zaBahlali okanye urhulumente wephondo okanye umasipala ) kunye nomhlaba onobunikazi babucala , ungangenelelwa ngokungekho mthethweni . .
Urhulumente unoxanduva lomgaqo lokuqinisekisa - xa kuyimfuneko , nangokusebenzisa izinto eziyimfuneko ezifumanekayo - ukuba bonke abemi banako ukuxhamla amalungelo abo asisiseko okufikelela kumhlaba nakwezezindlu okanye kwezezindlu . .
Xa kuqhubeke iimeko ezizodwa ezifana nokungenelelwa ngokuphangaleleyo nangokumandla kumhlaba othile , urhulumente ukwanoxanduva olufana nolu , lokuncedisa abanikazi bomhlaba babucala bakhusele umhlaba wabo . .
Xa abangeneleli bomhlaba abangekho mthethweni abanamalungelo asisiseko angekho mngciphekweni kufuneka bekhutshiwe , ugunyaziwe worhulumente onoxanduva lomhlaba wombuso obandakanyekayo okanye umnikazi womhlaba wabucala , kufuneka , ngaphandle kokulibazisa , acele inkundla ikhuphe umyalelo wokukhupha abangeneleli ngokoMthetho wokuThintela ukuKhutshwa okungekho Mthethweni kunye nokungenelela ngokungekho Mthethweni kuMhlaba othile , ekuthiwa yi of Illegal Eviction From and Unlawful Occupation of Land Act , 1998 . .
Lo mthetho xa kungoku ulawulwa liSebe lezeZindlu . .
Abantu ( kubandakanywa abangeneleli bomhlaba abangekho mthethweni ) , abangawufumaniyo umhlaba wezolimo , bangacela iSebe lezeMihlaba ukuze bancediswe bafumane umhlaba wezolimo ofanelekileyo . .
Abantu abadinga izindlu bangadibana nomasipala wendawo yabahlali , okanye , ukuba kuyimfuneko , iSebe lephondo okanye lelizwe lezeZindlu ukuze bancedwe . .
ISebe lezeMihlaba : .
liyakucela inkundla ikhuphe umyalelo wokukhupha abangeneleli abangekho mthethweni bomhlaba wombuso ophantsi kolawulo lwalo , solange amalungelo asisiseko abangeneleli abangekho mthethweni , engachaphazeleki .
liyakuncedisa abangeneleli abangekho mthethweni bawo nawuphina umhlaba wombuso okanye wabucala abadinga umhlaba wezolimo kwaye abangenawo umhlaba wezolimo bafikelele kumhlaba wezolimo ofanelekileyo .
liyakuncedisa abanye oogunyaziwe boorhulumente bafumanele abangeneleli abangekho mthethweni abadinga ezezindlu umhlaba ofanelekileyo ongomnye .
xa kuyimfuneko naxa kukho iimeko ezidinga uqwalaselo olulodwa , liyakuncedisa abanikazi babucala bomhlaba wezolimo abanomhlaba ongenelelwe ngokungekho mthethweni babeke abangeneleli abadinga umhlaba wezolimo kumhlaba ongomnyeofanelekileyo . .
Kwimeko apho umhlaba wabucala ungenelelwe ngokungekho mthethweni kwaye kungekho zimeko ezidinga uqwalaselo olulodwa , umnikazi womhlaba makacele inkundla , ngaphandle kokulibazisa , ikhuphe umyalelo wokukhutshwa kwabangeneleli ngokoMthetho wokuThintela ukuKhutshwa okungekho Mthethweni kunye nokungenelela ngokungekho Mthethweni kuMhlaba othile . .
Kwimeko apho umhlaba wabucala ungenelelwe ngokungekho mthethweni kwaye zikho iimeko ezidinga uqwalaselo olulodwa , umnikazi womhlaba angacela nayiphina i yeSebe lezeMihlaba ukuze ancedwe ukuba ngaba isizathu sesidingo sokungenelela kulo mhlaba kukufikelela kumhlaba wezolimo . .
Kwimeko apho umhlaba wabucala ungenelelwe ngokungekho mthethweni , kwaye zikho iimeko ezidinga uqwalaselo olulodwa , umnikazi womhlaba angacela umasipala wendawo yommandla , okanye , ukuba kuyimfuneko , iSebe lezeZindlu lephondo okanye lelizwe ukuze ancedwe ukuba ngaba isizathu sesidingo sokungenelela yimiba yezezindlu . .
Ukumisa ngokomthetho okanye ukugunyazisa amaxwebhu yinkqubo yokuqinisekiswa kwemisayino kwaye kuthetha ukuba amaxwebhu asemthethweni afakelwe , atywinwa kwaye asayiniwe nokuba kungeSiqinisekiso seApostille ( apho amazwe ayinxalenye yeNgqungquthela yaseHague yangomhla we kuOktobha 1961 ) , okanye ngoGunyaziso lwesiQinisekiso apho amazwe angeyonxalenye yeNgqungquthela yase Hague . .
ICandelo lokuMisa ngokomMthetho : .
limisa ngokusemthethweni amaxwebhu kawonke asemthethweni asayiniweyo ngaphakathi eMzantsi Afrika ukuze asetyenziswe ngaphandle kwemida yeRiphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika kusetyenziswa isiQinisekiso seApostille okanye IsiQinisekiso soGunyaziso .
linika abathengi izikhokelo zokufumana imisayino okanye amaxwebhu achanekilyo .
linika abathengi ulwazi ngemfono , ngeposi okanye nge . .
abameli beloMzantsi Afrika kwelaPhesheya banokumisa ngokomthetho amaxwebhu asemthethweni kuphela ukuba loo maxwebhu ebesele ' emiswe ngokomthetho ngaphambili ngosemaGunyeni wezangaPhandle ofanelekileyo okanye liCandelo eliMisa ngokusemThethweni kwiSebe lemiCimbi yezangaPhandle . .
Abameli beloMzantsi Afrika abanako ukukhupha isiQinisekiso seApostille - bangakhupha kuphela isiQinisekiso soGunyaziso . .
Okokuqala , qonda ukuba loluphi uxwebhu ofuna ukulumisa ngokusemthethweni . .
ICandelo lokuMisa ngokuseMthethweni lingakhupha isigunyaziso esifanelekileyo okanye isiQinisekiso seApostille ngokwale migaqo ilandelayo : .
Uxwebhu olo alukho ngaphezu konyaka ubudala . .
Kufuneka ulicebise iCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni malunga nelizwe apho luya kusetyenziswa khona olo xwebhu , ukuze libe nako ukufumanisa ukuba kufuneka iApostille okanye isiQinisekiso soGunyaziso na . .
Phambi kokuba iCandelo lokuMisa ngokuseMthethweni likhuphe isiGunyaziso okanye isiQinisekiso seApostlle esifanelekileyo , olo xwebhu kufuneka lumiswe ngokomthethweni : .
nguMantyi , uMantyi owoNgezelelweyo okanye uMantyi oNcedisayo .
nguMgcini okanye uMgcini oNcedisayo weNkundla ePhezulu yoMzantsi Afrika . .
Makungeniswe amaxwebhu kwiCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni ngokusebenzisa enye yezi ndlela zilandelayo : .
Asiwe ngumntu - Amaxwebhu angeniswe ngumntu angalandwa kuphela xa kukho ubungqina bokwamkelwa . .
Isiqinisekiso sokwamkelwa sinikwa wena emva kokunikezela amaxwebhu akho . .
Asiwe sisigidimi - Isigidimi siya kunikwa iphetshana lokuza kulanda , eliya kufunwa xa kulandwa amaxwebhu . .
Kufuneka usihlawule isigidimi xa sibuyisela amaxwebhu akho . .
Athunyelwe ngeposi ebhalisiweyo okanye ekhawulezayo - Kufuneka ufake imvulophu ebhalwe igama nedilesi yakho , ehlawulelweyo ( akwamkelwa mali ) nebukhulu bayo buyi ukuze iCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni likwazi ukuwabuyisa amaxwebhu . .
Ileta esisiqinisekiso , exela inani lamaxwebhu afuna ukumiswa ngokwasemthethweni , ilizwe ekufunelwa lona oku , kwakunye neenkcukacha zakho ezipheleleyo , kufuneka ihanjiswe kunye namaxwebhu . .
Kufuneka idlule kuMmeli weloMzantsi Afrika okwelaphesheya ( UmKhomishinala oPhezulu , uMzi woZakuzo okanye uMzi woMmeli ) . .
la maxwebhu alandelayo akamkelwa : .
Amaxwebhu afinyeziweyo okanye okubhalwe ngekhompyutha .
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zomtshato , zokuzalwa , zokufa okanye iziqinisekiso ezikhululayo zasemapoliseni .
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeziqinisekiso zoBume boMtshato ( akukho sithintelo ) okanye ubuNgqina bobuZwe .
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zamaxwebhu okundwendwela okanye iincwadi zezazisi .
Amaxwebhu aqinisekiswe ngabaKhomishinala beziFungo ukuba ziikopi zokwenyani zamaxwebhu akuqala . .
Umntu wasebuRhulumenteni onesiGunyaziso sokusayina kufuneka aqinisekise . .
la maxwebhu alandelayo akunyanzelekanga ukuba amiswe ngokusemthethweni yinkundla kuqala njengoko kuchaziwe ngentla apha , ngaphandle kokuba ebesayinwe ngumntu onegunya lokunikeza : .
Iziqinisekiso ezingafinyezwanga okanye ezipheleleyo zokuzalwa , zomtshato kunye / okanye ezokufa kunye neeleta eziqinisekisa ubume bobuzwe bomntu , ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitampu ngumqeshwa ogunyazisiweyo weSebe lemiCimbi yezeKhaya . .
Amaphepha okuthathela kuwe umntwana umkhulise asayiniweyo aze zagximfizwa isitampu nguMgcini wemicimbi yokuThathwa kwabantwana bakhuliswe ngabanye abazali kwiSebe lezoBulungisa . .
Amaxwebhu okuthumela ngaphandle kwelizwe asayiniweyo aze agximfizwa isitampu yiNdlu yezoRhwebo . .
Iziqinisekiso zemfundo ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitamptu ngumqeshwa ogunyazisiweyo kwiSebe lezeMfundo . .
Iziqinisekiso zokukhulula zamaPolisa ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitampu liZiko leNgxelo yolwaphulo leNkonzo yamaPolisa oMzantsi Afrika ( isiqinisekiso sokuKhulula samaPolisa sisemthethweni kwithuba leenyanga ezintathu kuphela ) . .
Ileta exela ukuba Akukho siThintelo ( ileta yobume bomtshato ) esayinwe yagximfizwa isitampu ngumqeshwa weSebe lemiCimbi yaseKhaya . .
Ubhaliso lwenkampani olusayinwe lwagximfizwa isitampu nguMgcini weenkampani eziluhlobo lwee Corporations . .
Iziqinisekiso zakwagqirha ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitampu ligosa eligunyazisiweyo kwiBhunga lemiSebenzi yezeMpilo . .
Amaxwebhu aphathelele kuthutho lwemfuyo , kuquka izilwanyana zasekhaya , kufuneka egximfizwe asayinwa nguGqirha weziLwanyana kaRhulumente . .
Xa kuthethwa ngenqanawa yokuloba yeli lizwe kubhekiswa kwinqanawa ( isikhephe ) ebhaliswe phantsi koMbuso weFlegi yaseMzantsi Afrika enikwe iSatifiketi soKhuseleko soGunyaziwe woKhuseleko loLwandle waseMzantsi Afrika , ekuthiwa yi African Maritime Safety Authority ( SAMSA ) kunye neLayisensi yeNqanawa yeSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho ekuthiwa yi of Environmental Affairs and Tourism ( DEA&T ) . .
Le nqanawa kufuneka : .
ibenobunikazi kwaye ilawulwe ngokupheleleyo ngumntu okanye abantu baseMzantsi Afrika , okanye .
ibenobunikazi kwaye ilawulwe ngokupheleleyo lilo naliphi na iqumrhu leenkampani , umbutho okanye naliphi na iqumrhu labantu elifakwe okanye elisekwe phantsi kwemithetho yeRiphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika , kwaye apho isininzi sezabelo kunye namalungelo okuvota alawulwa ngabantu baseMzantsi Afrika . .
Inqanawa yokuloba yeli lizwe idla ngokuxhotyiselwa ukuloba kunye neminye imisebenzi eyayamene nokuloba . .
Le nqanawa ibandakanya zonke izixhobo eziyimfuneko , izixhobo zokuloba , iindawo zokugcina imithwalo , umthwalo okanye iimpahla zorhwebo kunye namafutha alayishwe kuyo . .
Inqanawa yokuloba yeli lizwe ingabandakanya nayiphi na inqanawa encedisa enye okanye ezinye iinqanawa eziselwandle ekwenzeni nawuphi na umsebenzi owayamene nokuloba . .
Oku kungabandakanya ezi zinto zilandelayo , kodwa kungapheleli kuzo kuphela : .
amalungiselelo .
ukunika nokukhupha izinto eziyimfuneko .
indawo yokugcina imithwalo .
indawo yomkhenkce nokubandisa .
ukuthutha , okanye ukukhupha imveliso ; kunye / okanye .
nokwenza ngqo imisebenzi yokuloba kuMmandla oKhethekileyo wezoQoqosho ekuthiwa yi Economic Zone ( EEZ ) okanye kumanzi olwandle lwehlabathi phantsi kweflegi yeRiphablikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika . .
Akukho mntu unokusebenzisa inqanawa yokuloba okanye nayiphi na inqanawa ukuze asebenzise ilungelo lofikelelo , ngaphandle kokuba ikhutshiwe ilayisensi , enepemethe efanelekileyo ukuba ngaba umnikazi wenqanawa ngumntu onelungelo lokuloba . .
Kwimeko apho umnikazi wenqanawa engenalungelo lokuloba , kufuneka kubekho isivumelwano sekhontrakthi yokusebenzisa le nqanawa . .
Inqanawa yokuloba kufuneka iyokuvavanyelwa ukufanelana nolwandle ( yi ) kwaye i ingakhupha iSatifiketi soKhuseleko . .
Fumana ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho . .
Kufuneka ubengumntu onelungelo lokuloba ( ube wasenza isicelo selungelo lokuloba waze walinikwa elo lungelo ) . .
Ukubangaba akunalungelo lokuloba elingumnikazi wenqanawa , thumela okanye bandakanya isivumelwano sekhontrakthi , osingenele nomnikazi wenqanawa ukuze usebenzise le nqanawa kuthethwa ngayo , xa ufaka isicelo selayisensi yenqanawa . .
Thumela ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho nale nkcazelo ilandelayo : .
igama lenqanawa .
igama lomnikazi wale nqanawa .
uhlobo lwamandla , ubude benqanawa .
umlinganiselo wamandla e kunye nomlinganiselo womthwalo ongalingana kule nqanawa .
icandelo lokuloba ekujongwe ukuba le nqanawa isetyenziswe kulo .
uMbuso weFlegi ebhaliswe phantsi kwawo xa kungoku le nqanawa ( ukuba ngaba iqeshwe okanye kuvunyelwene ngayo ngekhontrakthi noMntu waseMzantsi Afrika oneLungelo lokuLoba ) . .
Zalisa le fom ngoonobumba abangadityaniswanga kwaye usebenzise oonobumba abakhulu kuphela , ufake nesiphakamiso esibhaliweyo esixhasa iimfuno zakho apho kuyimfuneko . .
Bonisa ixesha eya kulichitha le nqanawa kunye nendlela eya kusetyenziswa ngayo kwicandelo lokuloba eya kusebenza kulo . .
Injongo yale nkonzo kukulungiselela uluntu lukwazi ukufaka izikhalazo kwiCandelo loBuqondisi obuZimeleyo beZikhalazo , ekuthiwa yi Complaints Directorate ( ICD ) . .
Ukubangaba ufaka isikhalazo kwi yelizwe ye , umbandela uyakubhekiswa kwi ebandakanyekayo yephondo ( kuxhomekeke kummandla apho le nyewe yenzeke khona ) ukuze uphandwe . .
Iintlobo zezikhalazo ezingafakwa kwi : .
Isikhalazo soDidi II : Isikhalazo sokungalandeli kweNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika ngokoMthetho woBundlobongela baseKhaya ekuthiwa yi Violence Act , 1998 ngamanye amazwi ukuba ngaba ipolisa leNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika okanye likaMasipala aliphumelelanga ukuhambisana nemimiselo yoMthetho woBundlobongela baseKhaya . .
Isikhalazo soDidi III : Isikhalazo esityhola ukuba ipolisa okanye amapolisa abandakanyeka kwisenzo esigwenxa esikhokelele kulwenzakalo lomzimba olumasikizi oludinge unyango olungenisa isigulane esibhedlele . .
Oko kuziphatha kakubi okanye eso senzo sigwenxa kufuneka sibe senzeke ngexesha umntu eselugcinweni lwamapolisa . .
Le miba ilandelayo ludweliso lwezikhalazo zoDidi III : .
Ukusebenzisa kakubi amandla okunochaphazelo olubonakalayo kubahlali malunga nolwenzakalo olwenziweyo , inani labantu abachaphazelekayo , ubungakanani bemali ebandakanyekayo , isithuba sexesha eyenzeke ngalo . .
